uboot参考：
https://wiki.t-firefly.com/Firefly-RK3128/

配置交换内存：
# 1. 创建 swap 文件
sudo fallocate -l 16G /swapfile
# 如果 fallocate 不可用，可用：
# sudo dd if=/dev/zero of=/swapfile bs=1M count=16384

# 2. 设置权限（非常重要）
sudo chmod 600 /swapfile

# 3. 格式化为 swap
sudo mkswap /swapfile

# 4. 启用 swap
sudo swapon /swapfile

# 5. 验证
free -h







1.焊接sd卡槽，配置成从sd启动
2.接麦克风，接喇叭

K4B2G1646Q-BCKO K4B2G1646Q-BCK0 256MB DDR3内存芯片

解包流程：
mkdir test
cd test
dd if=../boot.img bs=1 skip=$((0x5C4000)) count=$((0x154C34)) of=ramdisk.gz  
gzip -d ramdisk.gz

mkdir ramdisk_root
cd ramdisk_root
sudo cpio -idmv < ../ramdisk

修改流程：

串口root:
service console /system/bin/sh
    class core
    console
    disabled
    user root
    group root
    seclabel u:r:init:s0




default.prop
-------------------
ro.secure=0
ro.debuggable=1
ro.adb.secure=0
persist.sys.usb.config=none


init.rc:
------------------
adb开启：
service adbd_tcp /sbin/adbd
    class main
    user root
    group root
    disabled
    seclabel u:r:adbd:s0
    oneshot

on property:sys.boot_completed=1
    #setprop service.adb.tcp.port 5555
    start adbd_tcp



sudo find . -print0 \
 | LC_ALL=C sort -z \
 | sudo cpio --null -o \
        -H newc \
        --owner=0:0 \
 > ../ramdisk.new

gzip -9 ramdisk.new

-------------------------------------------------------------

文件                            size

ramdisk.new.gz                  1,409,553  0x158211
                                1409553

                                1409863     0x158347
                                1409557     0x158215
                                1409552     0x158210  
                                1409556     0x158214
                                1409556     0x158214



1️解包 boot.img
2️解包 ramdisk
3️修改 default.prop（只改两行）
ro.debuggable=1
persist.sys.usb.config=adb
4️不要手动 chmod / chown（你之前问的那个问题，这里再次确认）
5️原样打包 ramdisk
6️重新打包 boot.img
1.需要winhex覆盖写入ramdisk部分
2.修改header中的ramdisk的大小
adb
在 init.rk30board.rc（不是 usb.rc）里：
找到：
on boot
在 这一段最后 加一行：
 setprop sys.usb.config adb

7️刷机
地址： 0x00014000   文件选择重新打包的boot.img
8 插 USB，adb devices


init.rc中写日志，可以通过串口或者 dmesg 看到
write /dev/kmsg "boot-init: starting adbd_tcp\n"







找到设备节点：
ls -la /dev/block/


dd命令：没有权限

dd if=/dev/block/rknand_uboot of=/sdcard/uboot.bin
/dev/block/rknand_uboot: cannot open for read: Permission denied


模拟器运行openwrt:
cd ~/openwrt/build_dir/target-arm_cortex-a7+neon-vfpv4_musl_eabi/linux-rockchip_armv7
qemu-system-arm \
  -M virt \
  -m 512M \
  -cpu cortex-a7 \
  -kernel Image \
  -dtb ~/openwrt/build_dir/target-arm_cortex-a7+neon-vfpv4_musl_eabi/linux-rockchip_armv7/image-rk3128-openwrt.dtb \
  -append "root=/dev/vda console=ttyAMA0 console=ttyS0 rw rootdelay=5" \
  -drive file=root.ext4,format=raw,if=virtio \
  -nographic \
  -serial mon:stdio


qemu-system-arm \
  -M virt \
  -m 512M \
  -cpu cortex-a7 \
  -kernel rk3128-initramfs-kernel.bin \
  -append "console=ttyAMA0 console=ttyS0 rw rootdelay=5" \
  -nographic \
  -serial mon:stdio


打包成安卓boot镜像：
./out/host/linux-x86/bin/mkbootimg
cd ~/openwrt
~/rk3128/out/host/linux-x86/bin/mkbootimg \
  --kernel rk3128-initramfs-kernel.bin \
  --ramdisk /dev/null \
  --cmdline "console=ttyFIQ0,115200 init=/init" \
  --base 0x60000000 \
  --pagesize 2048 \
  -o openwrt-rk3128-initramfs.img

编译新版uboot:
export CROSS_COMPILE=arm-linux-gnueabihf-
将uboot打包成miniloader.bin能用的
#./tools/boot_merger ./tools/rk_tools/RKBOOT/RK3128MINIALL.ini && \
#./tools/trust_merger --subfix ./tools/rk_tools/RKTRUST/RK3128TRUST.ini && \

resource也有格式的：

#define RESOURCE_PTN_HDR_MAGIC      "RSCE"
typedef struct {
	char     magic[4];//tag, "RSCE"
	uint16_t resource_ptn_version;
	uint16_t index_tbl_version;
	uint8_t  header_size;//blocks, size of ptn header.
	uint8_t  tbl_offset;//blocks, offset of index table.
	uint8_t  tbl_entry_size;//blocks, size of index table's entry.
	uint32_t tbl_entry_num;//numbers of index table's entry.
} resource_ptn_header;

#define INDEX_TBL_ENTR_TAG          "ENTR"
#define MAX_INDEX_ENTRY_PATH_LEN    256
typedef struct {
	char     tag[4];//tag, "ENTR"
	char     path[MAX_INDEX_ENTRY_PATH_LEN];
	uint32_t content_offset;//blocks, offset of resource content.
	uint32_t content_size;//bytes, size of resource content.
} index_tbl_entry;




#define FDT_MAGIC	0xd00dfeed	/* 4: version, 4: total size */
#define fdt_version(fdt)		(fdt_get_header(fdt, version))
//大端序
struct fdt_header {
	fdt32_t magic;			 /* magic word FDT_MAGIC */
	fdt32_t totalsize;		 /* total size of DT block */
	fdt32_t off_dt_struct;		 /* offset to structure */
	fdt32_t off_dt_strings;		 /* offset to strings */
	fdt32_t off_mem_rsvmap;		 /* offset to memory reserve map */
	fdt32_t version;		 /* format version */
	fdt32_t last_comp_version;	 /* last compatible version */

	/* version 2 fields below */
	fdt32_t boot_cpuid_phys;	 /* Which physical CPU id we're
					    booting on */
	/* version 3 fields below */
	fdt32_t size_dt_strings;	 /* size of the strings block */

	/* version 17 fields below */
	fdt32_t size_dt_struct;		 /* size of the structure block */
};


dt_struct 是一个 32-bit big-endian token 流，按深度优先遍历（DFS）顺序描述整棵设备树。

uint32_t token = FDT_BEGIN_NODE;
char     name[];        // 节点名字符串（\0 结尾）
padding                  // 4 字节对齐
注意：
name 是节点名（如 "soc@ff000000"）
根节点 name 是空字符串 ""
字符串结束后 必须补 0 填充到 4 字节对齐

uint32_t token = FDT_PROP;
uint32_t len;           // value 长度（字节）
uint32_t nameoff;       // 属性名在 dt_strings 中的偏移
uint8_t  value[len];    // 属性值原始数据
padding                  // 4 字节对齐
注意：
value 是裸数据：
<u32> → big-endian
string → \0 结尾
array → 连续字节

include/fdt.h
#ifndef __ASSEMBLY__
+--------------------+
| fdt_header         |
+--------------------+
| mem_rsvmap         |  
+--------------------+
| structure block    |
+--------------------+
| strings block      |
+--------------------+

令牌（宏定义）          数值	    含义	                                                    后续数据	                                                    对齐要求
FDT_BEGIN_NODE      0x00000001	标记一个节点开始	                                        节点的单元名称（以\0结尾的字符串）。根节点可以为空字符串。	        名称后需填充至4字节边界。
FDT_END_NODE	    0x00000002	标记一个节点结束	                                        无。	                                                       紧跟下一个令牌。
FDT_PROP	        0x00000003	标记一个属性的开始	                                        一个描述属性的结构体，后跟属性的值。	                          属性值后需填充至4字节边界。
FDT_NOP	            0x00000004	空操作，解析时被忽略，用于“删除”节点或属性而不移动数据。       无。	                                                          紧跟下一个令牌。
FDT_END	            0x00000009	标记整个Structure Block的结束。	                            无。	                                                       必须是结构块最后一个令牌。

struct fdt_header {
	fdt32_t magic;			 /* magic word FDT_MAGIC */
	fdt32_t totalsize;		 /* total size of DT block */
	fdt32_t off_dt_struct;		 /* offset to structure */
	fdt32_t off_dt_strings;		 /* offset to strings */
	fdt32_t off_mem_rsvmap;		 /* offset to memory reserve map */
	fdt32_t version;		 /* format version */
	fdt32_t last_comp_version;	 /* last compatible version */

	/* version 2 fields below */
	fdt32_t boot_cpuid_phys;	 /* Which physical CPU id we're
					    booting on */
	/* version 3 fields below */
	fdt32_t size_dt_strings;	 /* size of the strings block */

	/* version 17 fields below */
	fdt32_t size_dt_struct;		 /* size of the structure block */
};

struct fdt_reserve_entry {
	fdt64_t address;
	fdt64_t size;
};

struct fdt_node_header {
	fdt32_t tag;
	char name[0];
};

struct fdt_property {
	fdt32_t tag;
	fdt32_t len;
	fdt32_t nameoff;
	char data[0];
};

#endif /* !__ASSEMBLY */

#define FDT_MAGIC	0xd00dfeed	/* 4: version, 4: total size */
#define FDT_TAGSIZE	sizeof(fdt32_t)

#define FDT_BEGIN_NODE	0x1		/* Start node: full name */
#define FDT_END_NODE	0x2		/* End node */
#define FDT_PROP	0x3		/* Property: name off,
					   size, content */
#define FDT_NOP		0x4		/* nop */
#define FDT_END		0x9

修改如下：
--------------------------------------------------------
if [ -z "$DO_CHROOT" ]; then
maybe_break mount
log_begin_msg "Mounting root file system"

# ======== ADD HERE: wait for mmc root ========
case "${ROOT}" in
    /dev/mmcblk*|/dev/disk/by-*)
        echo "Waiting for root device ${ROOT} ..."
        i=0
        while [ ! -e "${ROOT}" ]; do
            sleep 0.2
            i=$((i+1))
            [ $i -ge 50 ] && break
        done
        ;;
esac
# ======== END ========

. /scripts/${BOOT}
parse_numeric ${ROOT}
maybe_break mountroot
mountroot
log_end_msg
fi

制作 initrd  ramdisk:
cd ~/rockchip-mkbootimg/initrd_root
sudo find . -print0 \
 | LC_ALL=C sort -z \
 | sudo cpio --null -o \
        -H newc \
        --owner=0:0 \
 > ../initrd.new
cd ~/rockchip-mkbootimg
gzip -9 initrd.new
truncate -s $(( ( $(stat -c%s initrd.new.gz) + 4 ) / 4 * 4 )) initrd.new.gz
cd ~/rockchip-mkbootimg/
mkbootimg --kernel ~/rk3128/kernel/arch/arm/boot/zImage --ramdisk initrd.new.gz -o linux-boot.img
cp linux-boot.img /mnt/f/rk3128/

uboot调用bootrk流程：
int do_bootrk(cmd_tbl_t *cmdtp, int flag, int argc, char * const argv[])
        ptn = get_disk_partition(boot_source);
        hdr = rk_load_image_from_storage(ptn, &images); //第一次加载ramdisk  kernel  fdt
                  kaddr = (void*)(unsigned long)CONFIG_KERNEL_LOAD_ADDR;
                  raddr = (void*)(gd->arch.rk_boot_buf_addr);    
                              #define CONFIG_KERNEL_LOAD_ADDR 	(CONFIG_RAM_PHY_START + SZ_32M)	/* 32M offset */
                              /*
                              *			Uboot memory map
                              *
                              * CONFIG_SYS_TEXT_BASE is the default address which maskrom loader uboot code.
                              * CONFIG_RKNAND_API_ADDR is the address which maskrom loader miniloader code.
                              *
                              *	kernel load address: CONFIG_SDRAM_PHY_START + 32M, size 16M,
                              *	miniloader code load address: CONFIG_SDRAM_PHY_START + 48M, size 8M,
                              *	total reverse memory is CONFIG_LMB_RESERVE_MEMORY_SIZE.
                              *
                              *|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|
                              *|START  -  KERNEL LOADER  -  NAND LOADER  -     LMB     -    Uboot    -  END|
                              *|SDRAM  -    START 32M    -   START 48M   -  START 56M  -  START 80M  - 128M|
                              *|       -     kernel      -   nand code   -     fdt     -   uboot/ramdisk   |
                              *|---------------------------------------------------------------------------|
                              */6000_0000   6200_0000        6300_0000      6380_0000      6500_0000    6800_0000
                
                if (StorageReadLba(ptn->start, (void *) hdr, 1 << 2) != 0) {
                  FBTERR("bootrk: failed to read bootimg header\n");
                  goto fail;
                }
                hdr->kernel_addr = (uint32)(unsigned long)kaddr;
                hdr->ramdisk_addr = (uint32)(unsigned long)raddr;
                
                // load kernel
                sector = ptn->start + (hdr->page_size / blksz);
                blocks = DIV_ROUND_UP(hdr->kernel_size, blksz);
                if (StorageReadLba(sector, (void *)(unsigned long) hdr->kernel_addr, blocks) != 0)
                
                // load ramdisk
                sector += ALIGN(hdr->kernel_size, hdr->page_size) / blksz;
                blocks = DIV_ROUND_UP(hdr->ramdisk_size, blksz);
                if (StorageReadLba(sector, (void *)(unsigned long) hdr->ramdisk_addr, blocks) != 0) 
                
                // load fdt
		            content = rkimage_load_fdt(get_disk_partition(RESOURCE_NAME));
                pimage->ft_addr = content.load_addr;
                pimage->ft_len = content.content_size;
                
                return hdr;
        
        rk_load_kernel_logo(); 
        rk_module_deinit(); // 通过 CRU（Clock & Reset Unit）寄存器把 I2C 控制器软复位,对 PL330 DMA 做 反初始化，确保 DMA 通道不再占用。
        SecureBootSecureState2Kernel(SecureBootCheckOK); //设置安全启动状态SecureBootCheckOK，0 关闭，1开启，从BootROM中获取的
        bootimg_print_image_hdr(hdr);
        printf("kernel   @ 0x%08x (0x%08x)\n", hdr->kernel_addr, hdr->kernel_size);
	      printf("ramdisk  @ 0x%08x (0x%08x)\n", hdr->ramdisk_addr, hdr->ramdisk_size);
        images.ep = hdr->kernel_addr;
        images.rd_start = hdr->ramdisk_addr;
        images.rd_end = hdr->ramdisk_addr + hdr->ramdisk_size;

        do_bootm_linux(0, 0, NULL, &images); // uboot 主线上的，Main Entry point for arm bootm implementation
                boot_prep_linux(images);
                        image_setup_linux(images);
                                // boot_fdt_add_mem_rsv_regions(lmb, *of_flat_tree);
                                        total = fdt_num_mem_rsv(fdt_blob);
                                        for (i = 0; i < total; i++) {
                                          if (fdt_get_mem_rsv(fdt_blob, i, &addr, &size) != 0)
                                            continue;
                                          printf("   reserving fdt memory region: addr=%llx size=%llx\n",
                                                (unsigned long long)addr, (unsigned long long)size);
                                          lmb_reserve(lmb, addr, size);
                                        }
                                // ret = boot_get_cmdline(lmb, &images->cmdline_start, &images->cmdline_end);
                                // 实际执行了，但是相关设置让他相当于没执行，只是标记保留了ramdisk的内存，ret = boot_ramdisk_high(lmb, images->rd_start, rd_len, initrd_start, initrd_end);  // relocate init ramdisk  第二次设置ramdisk的位置
                                        getenv: initrd_high = 0xffffffff=n  //从环境变量里设置了，不要搬移ramdisk
                                        debug("   in-place initrd\n");
                                        *initrd_start = rd_data;
                                        *initrd_end = rd_data + rd_len;
                                        lmb_reserve(lmb, rd_data, rd_len);
                                ret = boot_relocate_fdt(lmb, of_flat_tree, &of_size);
                                        of_start = (void *)(ulong) lmb_alloc_base(lmb, of_len, 0x200000, getenv_bootm_mapsize() + getenv_bootm_low());//原型：phys_addr_t lmb_alloc_base(struct lmb *lmb, phys_size_t size, phys_size_t align, phys_addr_t max_addr);
                                        debug("## device tree at %p ... %p (len=%ld [0x%lX])\n", fdt_blob, fdt_blob + *of_size - 1, of_len, of_len);
                                        printf("   Loading Device Tree to %p, end %p ... ", of_start, of_start + of_len - 1);
                                                ## device tree at 65753ec0 ... 65766a8b (len=89036 [0x15BCC])   //原来的内存地址
                                                Loading Device Tree to 65600000, end 65615bcb ... fdt_version >=17  //重定位到新的内存地址
                                        err = fdt_open_into(fdt_blob, of_start, of_len);
                                ret = image_setup_libfdt(images, *of_flat_tree, of_size, lmb);
                                        fdt_chosen(blob); // 就是把环境变量中设置的bootargs的值加到fdt的chosen/bootargs中
                                                nodeoffset = fdt_find_or_add_subnode(fdt, 0, "chosen");
                                                str = getenv("bootargs"); // 这个得加日志调试下，因为没看见哪里设置了这个环境变量
                                                bootargs = fdt_getprop(fdt, nodeoffset, "bootargs", NULL);
                                                snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "%s %s", bootargs, str);
                                                err = fdt_setprop(fdt, nodeoffset, "bootargs", buf, strlen(buf) + 1);
                                                return fdt_fixup_stdout(fdt, nodeoffset);
                                                        return 0;
                                        arch_fixup_fdt(blob); // 主要是设置内存硬件参数
                                        fdt_fixup_ethernet(blob); //设置网络
                                        /* Delete the old LMB reservation */
	                                      lmb_free(lmb, (phys_addr_t)(u32)(uintptr_t)blob, (phys_size_t)fdt_totalsize(blob)); //释放老的内存保留区域
                                        ret = fdt_shrink_to_minimum(blob); //收敛内存
                                        fdt_set_totalsize(blob, of_size); // of_size += FDT_RAMDISK_OVERHEAD; 为ramdisk在设备树中增加节点空间 if (*initrd_start && *initrd_end)
                                        lmb_reserve(lmb, (ulong)blob, of_size); // 设置新的保留内存区域
                                        fdt_initrd(blob, *initrd_start, *initrd_end); //1.在 mem_rsvmap 里保留 initrd 所占的物理内存； 2.在 /chosen 节点里写入 Linux 约定的 initrd 起止地址属性
                                                最终实现：/chosen {
                                                              linux,initrd-start = <...>;
                                                              linux,initrd-end   = <...>;
                                                          };
                                                          以及：mem_rsvmap:
                                                                [initrd_start, initrd_size]
                                                              → 告诉内核：这段内存不能回收
                                                nodeoffset = fdt_find_or_add_subnode(fdt, 0, "chosen");
                                                total = fdt_num_mem_rsv(fdt);  // 现在用的fdt保留内存部分好像是0，得加日志确认
                                                for (j = 0; j < total; j++) err = fdt_get_mem_rsv(fdt, j, &addr, &size);
                                                err = fdt_add_mem_rsv(fdt, initrd_start, initrd_end - initrd_start);

	              boot_jump_linux(images, flag);
                        ## Transferring control to Linux (at address 62000000)...
                        bootstage_mark(BOOTSTAGE_ID_RUN_OS); //uboot自己用来标记状态的，对内核没有功能影响
                        announce_and_cleanup(fake);
                                打印：
                                Starting kernel ...
                                清理 U-Boot 自己的环境：
                                关 console / serial flush
                                禁用 cache（部分平台）
                                关 watchdog
                                关中断
                                清理 malloc pool
                                如果 fake == 1：
                                  不真的跳内核
                                	可以理解为：“我要把机器交出去了”
                        kernel_entry(0, machid, r2);
                                CPU 从此属于 Linux

查一下这俩的区别
 CONFIG_BLK_DEV_RAM=y
 CONFIG_BLK_DEV_INITRD



 设备树中的“地址”，永远是“相对于父节点的地址空间”而言的。
 一个 cell = 32bit
 写法	地址宽度
#address-cells = <1>	32-bit 地址
#address-cells = <2>	64-bit 地址

-----------------------------------------
#address-cells = <2>;
#size-cells = <2>;

reg = <0x0 0x20064000  0x0 0x100>;
------------------------------------------

#define RK3036_UART2_PHYS		0x20068000
#define RK312X_UART2_PHYS               RK3036_UART2_PHYS


	uart2: serial@20068000 {
		compatible = "rockchip,serial";
		reg = <0x20068000 0x100>;
		interrupts = <GIC_SPI 22 IRQ_TYPE_LEVEL_HIGH>;
		clock-frequency = <24000000>;
		clocks = <&clk_uart2>, <&clk_gates8 2>;
		clock-names = "sclk_uart", "pclk_uart";
		reg-shift = <2>;
		reg-io-width = <4>;
		dmas = <&pdma 6>, <&pdma 7>;
		#dma-cells = <2>;
		pinctrl-names = "default";
		pinctrl-0 = <&uart2_xfer>;
		status = "disabled";
	};

uart3: serial@20068000 {
        compatible = "rockchip,serial";
        reg = <0x20068000 0x100>;
        interrupts = <GIC_SPI 37 IRQ_TYPE_LEVEL_HIGH>;
        clock-frequency = <24000000>;
        clocks = <&clk_uart3>, <&clk_gates8 3>;
        clock-names = "sclk_uart", "pclk_uart";
        reg-shift = <2>;
        reg-io-width = <4>;
        dmas = <&pdma1 8>, <&pdma1 9>;
        #dma-cells = <2>;
        pinctrl-names = "default";
        pinctrl-0 = <&uart3_xfer &uart3_cts &uart3_rts>;
        status = "disabled";
};

#!/bin/sh

mount -t proc proc /proc
mount -t sysfs sysfs /sys
mount -t devtmpfs devtmpfs /dev

echo "=== RK3128 initramfs init ==="

for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
    [ -e /dev/ttyS0 ] && break
    sleep 1
done

setsid sh -c '
    exec </dev/ttyS0 >/dev/ttyS0 2>&1
    echo
    echo "=== initramfs shell ready ==="
    echo "tty: /dev/ttyS0"
    echo
    exec /bin/cttyhack /bin/sh
'

//转换标准输入到控制台
// remote2console.c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <linux/input.h>
#include <sys/select.h>

// 按键码到控制台序列的映射
const char* get_console_sequence(int code, int value) {
    if (value != 1) return NULL;  // 只处理按下事件
    
    switch (code) {
        case KEY_UP:     return "\033[A";  // 上箭头
        case KEY_DOWN:   return "\033[B";  // 下箭头
        case KEY_RIGHT:  return "\033[C";  // 右箭头
        case KEY_LEFT:   return "\033[D";  // 左箭头
        case KEY_ENTER:  return "\n";
        case KEY_BACKSPACE: return "\b \b"; // 退格
        case KEY_0 ... KEY_9: {
            static char buf[2];
            buf[0] = '0' + (code - KEY_1 + 1);
            buf[1] = 0;
            return buf;
        }
        case KEY_A ... KEY_Z: {
            static char buf[2];
            buf[0] = 'a' + (code - KEY_A);
            buf[1] = 0;
            return buf;
        }
        default: return NULL;
    }
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
    int fd;
    struct input_event ev;
    const char *console = argc > 1 ? argv[1] : "/dev/console";
    
    // 打开输入设备
    fd = open("/dev/input/event0", O_RDONLY);
    if (fd < 0) {
        perror("open input");
        return 1;
    }
    
    // 打开控制台输出
    FILE *out = fopen(console, "w");
    if (!out) {
        perror("open console");
        close(fd);
        return 1;
    }
    
    printf("Remote to console bridge started. Press Ctrl+C to exit.\n");
    
    while (1) {
        if (read(fd, &ev, sizeof(ev)) != sizeof(ev)) {
            perror("read");
            break;
        }
        
        if (ev.type == EV_KEY) {
            const char *seq = get_console_sequence(ev.code, ev.value);
            if (seq) {
                fputs(seq, out);
                fflush(out);
            }
        }
    }
    
    fclose(out);
    close(fd);
    return 0;
}


export PATH=$HOME/gcc-linaro-arm-linux-gnueabi-2012.03-20120326_linux/bin:$PATH

//gpio用户空间操作
# 1. 查看有哪些 GPIO 控制器
ls /sys/class/gpio/
# 输出: export gpiochip0 gpiochip32 gpiochip64 gpiochip96 unexport

# 2. 计算 GPIO 编号（以 Rockchip 为例）
# GPIO4_C5 的计算公式: bank=4, 引脚C5=16+5=21 → 4*32 + 21 = 149
# 参考：GPIO_A0~A7=0-7, B0~B7=8-15, C0~C7=16-23, D0~D7=24-31 [citation:9]

# 3. 导出 GPIO
echo 8 > /sys/class/gpio/export

# 4. 设置方向为输出
echo "out" > /sys/class/gpio/gpio8/direction

# 5. 输出高电平
echo 1 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio8/value

# 6. 用完释放
echo 8 > /sys/class/gpio/unexport



////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
/*
 * remote_led_control.c
 * 功能：通过红外遥控控制GPIO LED
 * 左键 → 红灯（GPIO 8）亮/灭切换
 * 右键 → 蓝灯（GPIO 26）亮/灭切换
 * 
 * 编译：arm-linux-gnueabihf-gcc -static -o remote_led_control remote_led_control.c
 * 运行：./remote_led_control
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <errno.h>
#include <linux/input.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <signal.h>

// GPIO定义
#define RED_LED_GPIO     8    // 红灯引脚
#define BLUE_LED_GPIO    26   // 蓝灯引脚

// 按键码定义（来自linux/input-event-codes.h）
#define KEY_LEFT         105
#define KEY_RIGHT        106

// GPIO路径
#define GPIO_BASE_PATH   "/sys/class/gpio"
#define GPIO_EXPORT      GPIO_BASE_PATH "/export"
#define GPIO_UNEXPORT    GPIO_BASE_PATH "/unexport"

// LED状态
static int red_led_state = 0;   // 0=灭, 1=亮
static int blue_led_state = 0;

// 程序运行标志
static volatile int running = 1;

// 信号处理函数
void sigint_handler(int sig) {
    printf("\n接收到中断信号，正在清理并退出...\n");
    running = 0;
}

/**
 * 向文件写入字符串
 */
int write_to_file(const char *path, const char *value) {
    int fd = open(path, O_WRONLY);
    if (fd < 0) {
        printf("无法打开文件 %s: %s\n", path, strerror(errno));
        return -1;
    }
    
    int len = strlen(value);
    if (write(fd, value, len) != len) {
        printf("写入文件 %s 失败: %s\n", path, strerror(errno));
        close(fd);
        return -1;
    }
    
    close(fd);
    return 0;
}

/**
 * 导出GPIO
 */
int gpio_export(int gpio_num) {
    char gpio_str[8];
    snprintf(gpio_str, sizeof(gpio_str), "%d", gpio_num);
    
    printf("导出GPIO %d...\n", gpio_num);
    return write_to_file(GPIO_EXPORT, gpio_str);
}

/**
 * 设置GPIO方向
 */
int gpio_set_direction(int gpio_num, const char *direction) {
    char path[64];
    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), GPIO_BASE_PATH "/gpio%d/direction", gpio_num);
    
    printf("设置GPIO %d 方向为 %s...\n", gpio_num, direction);
    return write_to_file(path, direction);
}

/**
 * 设置GPIO输出值
 */
int gpio_set_value(int gpio_num, int value) {
    char path[64];
    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), GPIO_BASE_PATH "/gpio%d/value", gpio_num);
    
    char val_str[2] = {value ? '1' : '0', '\0'};
    return write_to_file(path, val_str);
}

/**
 * 取消导出GPIO
 */
int gpio_unexport(int gpio_num) {
    char gpio_str[8];
    snprintf(gpio_str, sizeof(gpio_str), "%d", gpio_num);
    
    printf("释放GPIO %d...\n", gpio_num);
    return write_to_file(GPIO_UNEXPORT, gpio_str);
}

/**
 * 初始化GPIO
 */
int init_gpio(void) {
    int ret;
    
    // 导出红灯GPIO
    ret = gpio_export(RED_LED_GPIO);
    if (ret < 0) {
        // 可能已经导出，继续尝试
        printf("GPIO %d 可能已经导出，继续...\n", RED_LED_GPIO);
    }
    
    // 等待sysfs节点创建
    usleep(100000);  // 100ms
    
    // 设置红灯方向为输出
    ret = gpio_set_direction(RED_LED_GPIO, "out");
    if (ret < 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "设置红灯GPIO方向失败\n");
        return -1;
    }
    
    // 初始状态：灭
    gpio_set_value(RED_LED_GPIO, 0);
    
    // 导出蓝灯GPIO
    ret = gpio_export(BLUE_LED_GPIO);
    if (ret < 0) {
        printf("GPIO %d 可能已经导出，继续...\n", BLUE_LED_GPIO);
    }
    
    // 等待sysfs节点创建
    usleep(100000);  // 100ms
    
    // 设置蓝灯方向为输出
    ret = gpio_set_direction(BLUE_LED_GPIO, "out");
    if (ret < 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "设置蓝灯GPIO方向失败\n");
        return -1;
    }
    
    // 初始状态：灭
    gpio_set_value(BLUE_LED_GPIO, 0);
    
    printf("GPIO初始化完成\n");
    return 0;
}

/**
 * 清理GPIO
 */
void cleanup_gpio(void) {
    printf("\n清理GPIO资源...\n");
    
    // 关闭LED
    gpio_set_value(RED_LED_GPIO, 0);
    gpio_set_value(BLUE_LED_GPIO, 0);
    
    // 取消导出（可选）
    gpio_unexport(RED_LED_GPIO);
    gpio_unexport(BLUE_LED_GPIO);
}

/**
 * 处理红外按键
 */
void handle_remote_key(int code, int value) {
    // 只处理按键按下事件（value=1）
    if (value != 1) {
        return;
    }
    
    switch (code) {
        case KEY_LEFT:
            // 左键：切换红灯状态
            red_led_state = !red_led_state;
            gpio_set_value(RED_LED_GPIO, red_led_state);
            printf("红灯 %s\n", red_led_state ? "亮" : "灭");
            break;
            
        case KEY_RIGHT:
            // 右键：切换蓝灯状态
            blue_led_state = !blue_led_state;
            gpio_set_value(BLUE_LED_GPIO, blue_led_state);
            printf("蓝灯 %s\n", blue_led_state ? "亮" : "灭");
            break;
            
        default:
            // 其他按键忽略
            break;
    }
}

int main(int argc, char **argv) {
    int fd;
    struct input_event ev;
    fd_set fds;
    struct timeval timeout;
    int ret;
    
    // 设置信号处理，以便Ctrl+C时清理
    signal(SIGINT, sigint_handler);
    
    printf("红外遥控LED控制程序启动\n");
    printf("左键：控制红灯\n");
    printf("右键：控制蓝灯\n");
    printf("按Ctrl+C退出\n\n");
    
    // 初始化GPIO
    if (init_gpio() < 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "GPIO初始化失败\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    // 打开输入设备
    fd = open("/dev/input/event0", O_RDONLY);
    if (fd < 0) {
        fprintf(stderr, "无法打开 /dev/input/event0: %s\n", strerror(errno));
        fprintf(stderr, "请检查输入设备是否存在\n");
        cleanup_gpio();
        return 1;
    }
    
    printf("开始监听红外遥控...\n");
    
    // 主循环
    while (running) {
        FD_ZERO(&fds);
        FD_SET(fd, &fds);
        
        timeout.tv_sec = 1;      // 1秒超时
        timeout.tv_usec = 0;
        
        ret = select(fd + 1, &fds, NULL, NULL, &timeout);
        
        if (ret < 0) {
            if (errno == EINTR) {
                continue;  // 被信号中断
            }
            perror("select错误");
            break;
        }
        
        if (ret == 0) {
            // 超时，继续循环（可用于添加其他功能）
            continue;
        }
        
        if (FD_ISSET(fd, &fds)) {
            // 读取输入事件
            int bytes = read(fd, &ev, sizeof(ev));
            
            if (bytes == sizeof(ev)) {
                // 只处理按键事件
                if (ev.type == EV_KEY) {
                    handle_remote_key(ev.code, ev.value);
                }
            } else if (bytes < 0) {
                if (errno != EINTR) {
                    perror("读取事件错误");
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // 清理
    close(fd);
    cleanup_gpio();
    
    printf("程序退出\n");
    return 0;
}


----------------------------------------------------------------------

framebuffer

---

# 一、先建立“显示全路径”架构模型

在 RK3128 上，从内存到 HDMI 显示的路径大致是：

```
用户空间 (C 程序)
        ↓
framebuffer / DRM
        ↓
DRM/KMS 框架
        ↓
VOP (Video Output Processor)
        ↓
HDMI Controller
        ↓
HDMI PHY
        ↓
TMDS 差分信号
        ↓
显示器
```

GPU（Mali-400）只是做 3D/合成加速，不是必须。

现在的目标：

不用 GPU，直接用 framebuffer 输出
理解 Linux DRM 框架
理解 Rockchip VOP + HDMI 控制器
最终自己用 C 画像素

---

确认现在的内核状态


* u-boot 
* kernel
* busybox initramfs 
* 无图形 

先确认：

```bash
zcat /proc/config.gz | grep DRM
```

如果没有开启：

```
CONFIG_DRM=y
CONFIG_DRM_ROCKCHIP=y
CONFIG_DRM_ROCKCHIP_VOP=y
CONFIG_DRM_ROCKCHIP_DW_HDMI=y
```

你需要重新开启。

---

理解 Linux 显示子系统结构

重点研究：

DRM 框架（核心）

源码目录：

```
drivers/gpu/drm/
```

必读：

```
drm_drv.c
drm_mode_config.c
drm_crtc.c
drm_connector.c
drm_encoder.c
```

理解 4 个概念：

| 组件        | 作用                |
| --------- | ----------------- |
| CRTC      | 扫描 framebuffer 输出 |
| Encoder   | 信号编码（RGB→TMDS）    |
| Connector | 物理接口（HDMI）        |
| Plane     | 图层                |

---

2️Rockchip 显示驱动

目录：

```
drivers/gpu/drm/rockchip/
```

重点看：

```
rockchip_drm_drv.c
rockchip_vop.c
```

VOP = Video Output Processor
这是 RK3128 的显示控制器。

---

3️ HDMI 控制器

RK3128 用的是 Synopsys 的 DesignWare HDMI IP。

驱动在：

```
drivers/gpu/drm/bridge/synopsys/dw-hdmi.c
```

Rockchip glue：

```
dw_hdmi-rockchip.c
```

这两部分是核心。

---

设备树

你必须理解 dts。

查找：

```
arch/arm/boot/dts/rk3128.dtsi
```

重点节点：

```dts
vop: vop@...
hdmi: hdmi@...
```

以及：

```
&hdmi {
    status = "okay";
};
```

如果 HDMI 没开，驱动根本不会 probe。

---

硬件层理解

你必须理解 RK3128 的显示模块结构：

```
DDR → AXI → VOP → HDMI Controller → PHY
```

重点：

* VOP 负责：

  * 从 DDR 读取 framebuffer
  * 做 scaling
  * 做 color convert
  * 生成 timing
* HDMI Controller 负责：

  * EDID 读取
  * TMDS 编码
  * 视频模式设置

RK3128 TRM（Technical Reference Manual）

重点章节：

* VOP 寄存器
* HDMI 寄存器
* GRF (General Register Files)

---

学习顺序


---

1：只用 framebuffer 输出

打开：

```
CONFIG_FB_SIMPLE=y
```

让 U-Boot 传递 framebuffer。

然后在用户态：

```c
int fd = open("/dev/fb0", O_RDWR);
mmap(...)
memset(...)
```

测试能否点亮屏幕。

如果成功：

你已经打通：

```
DDR → VOP → HDMI → 显示器
```

---

 2：启用 DRM + KMS

关闭 simplefb

打开：

```
CONFIG_DRM_ROCKCHIP
CONFIG_DRM_FBDEV_EMULATION
```

启动后：

```
/dev/dri/card0
```

测试：

```
modetest -M rockchip
```

看到：

* connector
* encoder
* crtc
* mode

---

3：阅读 rockchip_vop.c

重点理解：

```c
vop_enable()
vop_crtc_atomic_enable()
vop_plane_atomic_update()
```

核心就是：

```
写寄存器
设置 timing
启动扫描
```

写 C 版 Flappy Bird

1. mmap framebuffer
2. 写一个 2D 像素绘制库
3. 写一个定时器循环
4. 用你现在的红外输入事件
5. 刷新 framebuffer

核心函数：

```c
void draw_pixel(x,y,color)
void draw_rect(...)
void draw_bitmap(...)
```

然后：

```
while (1) {
    read_remote();
    update_game_state();
    render();
}
```

EDID: Extended Display Identification Data
信息类别	具体内容
制造商信息	厂商名称、产品ID、生产日期
基本参数	屏幕尺寸、宽高比、支持的最大分辨率
支持的分辨率	所有支持的显示模式（如 1080p60、720p50、480i 等）
时序参数	每个分辨率对应的详细时序（HFP、HBP、VFP、VBP）
物理特性	屏幕类型（LCD、OLED）、色彩深度、色域
音频能力	是否支持音频、支持的音频格式（如 LPCM、AC-3）
3D 支持	是否支持 3D 显示
HDMI 特性	支持的 HDMI 版本、HDCP 支持情况

3. EDID 的物理存储
通常存储在显示器内部的 EEPROM（电可擦可编程只读存储器）中

容量一般为 128字节（基础版本）或 256字节（扩展版本）


UBOOT 中 HDMI 硬件初始化流程
rk3036_hdmi_hardware_init

hdmi_detect_hotplug


开启HDMI调试模式：
include\configs\rk30plat.h 中添加
#define HDMIDEBUG

1366 * 768

HDMI:       70 MHz 
HDMI: 1366 1414 1446 1500 
HDMI: 768 771 774 780 
HDMI: +HSync +VSync



Byte  Description
------------------------------------------------
0-1   Pixel Clock (2 bytes)

2     H Active (LSB)
3     H Blanking (LSB)

4     H Active[11:8] | H Blanking[11:8]

5     V Active (LSB)
6     V Blanking (LSB)

7     V Active[11:8] | V Blanking[11:8]

8     H Sync Offset (LSB)
9     H Sync Pulse Width (LSB)

10    V Sync Offset[3:0] | V Sync Width[3:0]

11    H Sync Offset[9:8] | H Sync Width[9:8]
      | V Sync Offset[5:4] | V Sync Width[5:4]

12    Horizontal Image Size (LSB)
13    Vertical Image Size (LSB)

14    H Image Size[11:8] | V Image Size[11:8]

15    H Border

16    V Border

17    Flags



| 字节范围   | 内容                          |
| ------ | --------------------------- |
| 0–7    | Header                      |
| 8–9    | Manufacturer ID             |
| 10–11  | Product Code                |
| 12–15  | Serial Number               |
| 16     | Manufacture Week            |
| 17     | Manufacture Year            |
| 18     | EDID Version                |
| 19     | EDID Revision               |
| 20–24  | Basic Display Parameters    |
| 25–34  | Color Characteristics       |
| 35–37  | Established Timings         |
| 38–53  | Standard Timings            |
| 54–125 | Detailed Timing Descriptors |
| 126    | Extension Block Count       |
| 127    | Checksum                    |


Standard Timing
总共 16 字节 = 8 个时序描述符，
每个时序占 2 字节。
Byte1: Horizontal Active Pixels
Byte2: Aspect Ratio + Refresh Rate

bit7-6 : Aspect Ratio
bit5-0 : Refresh Rate

| bit7-6 | 宽高比   |
| ------ | ----- |
| 00     | 16:10 |
| 01     | 4:3   |
| 10     | 5:4   |
| 11     | 16:9  |


Refresh Rate = (bits[5:0]) + 60



| tag  | 含义                       |
| ---- | ------------------------ |
| 0xFF | Monitor Serial Number    |
| 0xFE | ASCII text               |
| 0xFC | Monitor Name             |
| 0xFD | Monitor Range            |
| 0xFA | Display Standard Timings |

// slideshow.c
static int abortboot_normal(int bootdelay)
{
	int abort = 0;
	unsigned long ts;

#ifdef CONFIG_MENUPROMPT
	printf(CONFIG_MENUPROMPT);
#else
	if (bootdelay >= 0)
		printf("Hit any key to stop autoboot: %2d ", bootdelay);
#endif

#if defined CONFIG_ZERO_BOOTDELAY_CHECK
	/*
	 * Check if key already pressed
	 * Don't check if bootdelay < 0
	 */
	if (bootdelay >= 0) {
		if (tstc()) {	/* we got a key press	*/
			(void) getc();  /* consume input	*/
			puts("\b\b\b 0");
			abort = 1;	/* don't auto boot	*/
		}
	}
#endif

	while ((bootdelay > 0) && (!abort)) {
		--bootdelay;
		/* delay 1000 ms */
		ts = get_timer(0);
		do {
			if (tstc()) {	/* we got a key press	*/
				abort  = 1;	/* don't auto boot	*/
				bootdelay = 0;	/* no more delay	*/
# ifdef CONFIG_MENUKEY
				menukey = getc();
# else
				(void) getc();  /* consume input	*/
# endif
				break;
			}
			udelay(10000);
		} while (!abort && get_timer(ts) < 1000);

		printf("\b\b\b%2d ", bootdelay);
	}

	putc('\n');

#ifdef CONFIG_SILENT_CONSOLE
	if (abort)
		gd->flags &= ~GD_FLG_SILENT;
#endif

	return abort;
}

/************************************************************************/
/* ** CONSOLE DEFINITIONS & FUNCTIONS					*/
/************************************************************************/
#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
#if defined(CONFIG_LCD_LOGO) && !defined(CONFIG_LCD_INFO_BELOW_LOGO)
# define CONSOLE_ROWS		((panel_info.vl_row-BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT) \
					/ VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT)
#else
# define CONSOLE_ROWS		(panel_info.vl_row / VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT)
#endif

#define CONSOLE_COLS		(panel_info.vl_col / VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH)
#define CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE	(VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT * lcd_line_length)
#define CONSOLE_ROW_FIRST	lcd_console_address
#define CONSOLE_ROW_SECOND	(lcd_console_address + CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE)
#define CONSOLE_ROW_LAST	(lcd_console_address + CONSOLE_SIZE \
					- CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE)
#define CONSOLE_SIZE		(CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * CONSOLE_ROWS)
#define CONSOLE_SCROLL_SIZE	(CONSOLE_SIZE - CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE)
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

#if (LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR8) || (LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR16) || \
	(LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR32)
# define COLOR_MASK(c)		(c)
#else
# error Unsupported LCD BPP.
#endif

DECLARE_GLOBAL_DATA_PTR;

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
static void lcd_drawchars(ushort x, ushort y, uchar *str, int count);
static inline void lcd_putc_xy(ushort x, ushort y, uchar  c);
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

static int lcd_init(void *lcdbase);

static void *lcd_logo(void);

static void lcd_setfgcolor(int color);
static void lcd_setbgcolor(int color);

static int lcd_color_fg;
static int lcd_color_bg;
int lcd_line_length;

char lcd_is_enabled = 0;
#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
char lcd_show_logo = 0;
bool lcd_flip = false;

extern void lcd_pandispaly(struct fb_dsp_info *info);
#endif

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
static short console_col;
static short console_row;
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

static void *lcd_console_address;
static void *lcd_base;			/* Start of framebuffer memory	*/

static char lcd_flush_dcache;	/* 1 to flush dcache after each lcd update */


static int gx = 0, gy = 0;
static int gwidth = 0, gheight = 0;
static int g_format = 0;
/************************************************************************/

/* Flush LCD activity to the caches */
void lcd_sync(void)
{
	/*
	 * flush_dcache_range() is declared in common.h but it seems that some
	 * architectures do not actually implement it. Is there a way to find
	 * out whether it exists? For now, ARM is safe.
	 */
#if defined(CONFIG_ARM) && !defined(CONFIG_SYS_DCACHE_OFF)
	int line_length;

	if (lcd_flush_dcache)
		flush_dcache_range((u32)(unsigned long)lcd_base,
			(u32)(unsigned long)(lcd_base + lcd_get_size(&line_length)));
#elif defined(CONFIG_SANDBOX) && defined(CONFIG_VIDEO_SANDBOX_SDL)
	static ulong last_sync;

	if (get_timer(last_sync) > 10) {
		sandbox_sdl_sync(lcd_base);
		last_sync = get_timer(0);
	}
#endif
}

void lcd_set_flush_dcache(int flush)
{
	lcd_flush_dcache = (flush != 0);
}

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static void console_scrollup(void)
{
	const int rows = CONFIG_CONSOLE_SCROLL_LINES;

	/* Copy up rows ignoring those that will be overwritten */
	memcpy(CONSOLE_ROW_FIRST,
	       lcd_console_address + CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows,
	       CONSOLE_SIZE - CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows);

	/* Clear the last rows */
#if (LCD_BPP != LCD_COLOR32)
	memset(lcd_console_address + CONSOLE_SIZE - CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows,
		COLOR_MASK(lcd_color_bg),
		CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows);
#else
	u32 *ppix = lcd_console_address +
		    CONSOLE_SIZE - CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows;
	u32 i;
	for (i = 0;
	    i < (CONSOLE_ROW_SIZE * rows) / NBYTES(panel_info.vl_bpix);
	    i++) {
		*ppix++ = COLOR_MASK(lcd_color_bg);
	}
#endif
	lcd_sync();
	console_row -= rows;
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static inline void console_back(void)
{
	if (--console_col < 0) {
		console_col = CONSOLE_COLS-1 ;
		if (--console_row < 0)
			console_row = 0;
	}

	lcd_putc_xy(console_col * VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
		console_row * VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT, ' ');
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static inline void console_newline(void)
{
	console_col = 0;

	/* Check if we need to scroll the terminal */
	if (++console_row >= CONSOLE_ROWS)
		console_scrollup();
	else
		lcd_sync();
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static void lcd_stub_putc(struct stdio_dev *dev, const char c)
{
	lcd_putc(c);
}

void lcd_putc(const char c)
{
	if (!lcd_is_enabled) {
		serial_putc(c);

		return;
	}

	switch (c) {
	case '\r':
		console_col = 0;

		return;
	case '\n':
		console_newline();

		return;
	case '\t':	/* Tab (8 chars alignment) */
		console_col +=  8;
		console_col &= ~7;

		if (console_col >= CONSOLE_COLS)
			console_newline();

		return;
	case '\b':
		console_back();

		return;
	default:
		lcd_putc_xy(console_col * VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH,
			console_row * VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT, c);
		if (++console_col >= CONSOLE_COLS)
			console_newline();
	}
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static void lcd_stub_puts(struct stdio_dev *dev, const char *s)
{
	lcd_puts(s);
}

void lcd_puts(const char *s)
{
	if (!lcd_is_enabled) {
		serial_puts(s);

		return;
	}

	while (*s)
		lcd_putc(*s++);

	lcd_sync();
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

void lcd_printf(const char *fmt, ...)
{
	va_list args;
	char buf[CONFIG_SYS_PBSIZE];

	va_start(args, fmt);
	vsprintf(buf, fmt, args);
	va_end(args);

	lcd_puts(buf);
}

/************************************************************************/
/* ** Low-Level Graphics Routines					*/
/************************************************************************/

static void lcd_drawchars(ushort x, ushort y, uchar *str, int count)
{
	uchar *dest;
	ushort row;

#if defined(CONFIG_LCD_LOGO) && !defined(CONFIG_LCD_INFO_BELOW_LOGO)
	y += BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT;
#endif

	dest = (uchar *)(lcd_base + y * lcd_line_length + x * NBITS(LCD_BPP)/8);

	for (row = 0; row < VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT; ++row, dest += lcd_line_length) {
		uchar *s = str;
		int i;
#if LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR16
		ushort *d = (ushort *)dest;
#elif LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR32
		u32 *d = (u32 *)dest;
#else
		uchar *d = dest;
#endif

		for (i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
			uchar c, bits;

			c = *s++;
			bits = video_fontdata[c * VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT + row];

			for (c = 0; c < 8; ++c) {
				*d++ = (bits & 0x80) ?
						lcd_color_fg : lcd_color_bg;
				bits <<= 1;
			}
		}
	}
}

static inline void lcd_putc_xy(ushort x, ushort y, uchar c)
{
	lcd_drawchars(x, y, &c, 1);
}
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

/************************************************************************/
/**  Small utility to check that you got the colours right		*/
/************************************************************************/
#ifdef LCD_TEST_PATTERN

#define	N_BLK_VERT	2
#define	N_BLK_HOR	3

static int test_colors[N_BLK_HOR * N_BLK_VERT] = {
	CONSOLE_COLOR_RED,	CONSOLE_COLOR_GREEN,	CONSOLE_COLOR_YELLOW,
	CONSOLE_COLOR_BLUE,	CONSOLE_COLOR_MAGENTA,	CONSOLE_COLOR_CYAN,
};

static void test_pattern(void)
{
	ushort v_max  = panel_info.vl_row;
	ushort h_max  = panel_info.vl_col;
	ushort v_step = (v_max + N_BLK_VERT - 1) / N_BLK_VERT;
	ushort h_step = (h_max + N_BLK_HOR  - 1) / N_BLK_HOR;
	ushort v, h;
	uchar *pix = (uchar *)lcd_base;

	printf("[LCD] Test Pattern: %d x %d [%d x %d]\n",
		h_max, v_max, h_step, v_step);

	/* WARNING: Code silently assumes 8bit/pixel */
	for (v = 0; v < v_max; ++v) {
		uchar iy = v / v_step;
		for (h = 0; h < h_max; ++h) {
			uchar ix = N_BLK_HOR * iy + h / h_step;
			*pix++ = test_colors[ix];
		}
	}
}
#endif /* LCD_TEST_PATTERN */


/************************************************************************/
/* ** GENERIC Initialization Routines					*/
/************************************************************************/
/*
 * With most lcd drivers the line length is set up
 * by calculating it from panel_info parameters. Some
 * drivers need to calculate the line length differently,
 * so make the function weak to allow overriding it.
 */
__weak int lcd_get_size(int *line_length)
{
	*line_length = (panel_info.vl_col * NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix)) / 8;
	return *line_length * panel_info.vl_row;
}

#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
void lcd_enable_logo(bool enable)
{
	lcd_show_logo = enable;
	//if (lcd_show_logo)
	//	lcd_clear();
}

void lcd_enable_flip(bool enable)
{
	lcd_flip = enable;
}
#endif

int drv_lcd_init(void)
{
	printf("[LCD] Initializing\n");
	struct stdio_dev lcddev;
	int rc;

	lcd_base = map_sysmem(gd->fb_base, 0);

	lcd_init(lcd_base);		/* LCD initialization */

	/* Device initialization */
	memset(&lcddev, 0, sizeof(lcddev));

	strcpy(lcddev.name, "lcd");
	lcddev.ext   = 0;			/* No extensions */
#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
	lcddev.flags = DEV_FLAGS_OUTPUT;	/* Output only */
	lcddev.putc  = lcd_stub_putc;		/* 'putc' function */
	lcddev.puts  = lcd_stub_puts;		/* 'puts' function */
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

	rc = stdio_register(&lcddev);

	return (rc == 0) ? 1 : rc;
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
void lcd_clear(void)
{
#if LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR8
	/* Setting the palette */
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_BLACK, 0, 0, 0);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_RED, 0xFF, 0, 0);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_GREEN, 0, 0xFF, 0);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_YELLOW, 0xFF, 0xFF, 0);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_BLUE, 0, 0, 0xFF);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_MAGENTA, 0xFF, 0, 0xFF);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_CYAN, 0, 0xFF, 0xFF);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_GREY, 0xAA, 0xAA, 0xAA);
	lcd_setcolreg(CONSOLE_COLOR_WHITE, 0xFF, 0xFF, 0xFF);
#endif

#ifndef CONFIG_SYS_WHITE_ON_BLACK
	lcd_setfgcolor(CONSOLE_COLOR_BLACK);
	lcd_setbgcolor(CONSOLE_COLOR_WHITE);
#else
	lcd_setfgcolor(CONSOLE_COLOR_WHITE);
	lcd_setbgcolor(CONSOLE_COLOR_BLACK);
#endif	/* CONFIG_SYS_WHITE_ON_BLACK */

#ifdef	LCD_TEST_PATTERN
	test_pattern();
#else
	/* set framebuffer to background color */
#if (LCD_BPP != LCD_COLOR32)
	memset((char *)lcd_base,
		COLOR_MASK(lcd_color_bg),
		lcd_line_length * panel_info.vl_row);
#else
	u32 *ppix = lcd_base;
	u32 i;
	for (i = 0;
	   i < (lcd_line_length * panel_info.vl_row)/NBYTES(panel_info.vl_bpix);
	   i++) {
		*ppix++ = COLOR_MASK(lcd_color_bg);
	}
#endif
#endif
	/* Paint the logo and retrieve LCD base address */

#ifndef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
	debug("[LCD] Drawing the logo...\n");
	lcd_console_address = lcd_logo();
#else
	if (lcd_show_logo)
	{
		debug("[LCD] Drawing the logo...\n");
		lcd_console_address = lcd_logo();
	}
#endif

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
	console_col = 0;
	console_row = 0;
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */
	lcd_sync();
}

static int do_lcd_clear(cmd_tbl_t *cmdtp, int flag, int argc,
			char *const argv[])
{
	lcd_clear();
	return 0;
}

U_BOOT_CMD(
	cls,	1,	1,	do_lcd_clear,
	"clear screen",
	""
);

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static int lcd_init(void *lcdbase)
{
	/* Initialize the lcd controller */
	debug("[LCD] Initializing LCD frambuffer at %p\n", lcdbase);

	lcd_ctrl_init(lcdbase);

	/*
	 * lcd_ctrl_init() of some drivers (i.e. bcm2835 on rpi_b) ignores
	 * the 'lcdbase' argument and uses custom lcd base address
	 * by setting up gd->fb_base. Check for this condition and fixup
	 * 'lcd_base' address.
	 */
	if (map_to_sysmem(lcdbase) != gd->fb_base)
		lcd_base = map_sysmem(gd->fb_base, 0);

	debug("[LCD] Using LCD frambuffer at %p\n", lcd_base);

	lcd_get_size(&lcd_line_length);
	lcd_is_enabled = 1;
#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
	lcd_flip = false;
#endif
	lcd_clear();
	lcd_enable();

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
	/* Initialize the console */
	console_col = 0;
#ifdef CONFIG_LCD_INFO_BELOW_LOGO
	console_row = 7 + BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT / VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT;
#else
	console_row = 1;	/* leave 1 blank line below logo */
#endif
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

	return 0;
}


/************************************************************************/
/* ** ROM capable initialization part - needed to reserve FB memory	*/
/************************************************************************/
/*
 * This is called early in the system initialization to grab memory
 * for the LCD controller.
 * Returns new address for monitor, after reserving LCD buffer memory
 *
 * Note that this is running from ROM, so no write access to global data.
 */
ulong lcd_setmem(ulong addr)
{
	ulong size;
	int line_length;

	debug("LCD panel info: %d x %d, %d bit/pix\n", panel_info.vl_col,
		panel_info.vl_row, NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix));

	size = lcd_get_size(&line_length);

	/* Round up to nearest full page, or MMU section if defined */
	size = ALIGN(size, CONFIG_LCD_ALIGNMENT);
	addr = ALIGN(addr - CONFIG_LCD_ALIGNMENT + 1, CONFIG_LCD_ALIGNMENT);

	/* Allocate pages for the frame buffer. */
	addr -= size;

	debug("Reserving %ldk for LCD Framebuffer at: %08lx\n",
	      size >> 10, addr);

	return addr;
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static void lcd_setfgcolor(int color)
{
	lcd_color_fg = color;
}

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/

static void lcd_setbgcolor(int color)
{
	lcd_color_bg = color;
}

/************************************************************************/
/* ** Chipset depending Bitmap / Logo stuff...                          */
/************************************************************************/
static inline ushort *configuration_get_cmap(void)
{
#if defined CONFIG_CPU_PXA
	struct pxafb_info *fbi = &panel_info.pxa;
	return (ushort *)fbi->palette;
#elif defined(CONFIG_MPC823)
	immap_t *immr = (immap_t *) CONFIG_SYS_IMMR;
	cpm8xx_t *cp = &(immr->im_cpm);
	return (ushort *)&(cp->lcd_cmap[255 * sizeof(ushort)]);
#elif defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD)
	return (ushort *)(panel_info.mmio + ATMEL_LCDC_LUT(0));
#elif !defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_HLCD) && !defined(CONFIG_EXYNOS_FB) && !defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
	return panel_info.cmap;
#elif defined(CONFIG_LCD_LOGO)
	return bmp_logo_palette;
#else
	return NULL;
#endif
}

#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
#include <resource.h>
int rk_bitmap_from_resource(unsigned short* fb) 
{
	const char* file_path = "logo.bmp";
	return show_resource_image(file_path) ? 0 : -1;
}
#endif

#if defined(CONFIG_LCD_LOGO)

void bitmap_plot(int x, int y)
{
#ifdef CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD
	uint *cmap = (uint *)bmp_logo_palette;
#else
	ushort *cmap = (ushort *)bmp_logo_palette;
#endif
	ushort i, j;
	uchar *bmap;
	uchar *fb;
	ushort *fb16;
#if defined(CONFIG_MPC823)
	immap_t *immr = (immap_t *) CONFIG_SYS_IMMR;
	cpm8xx_t *cp = &(immr->im_cpm);
#endif
	unsigned bpix = NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix);

	debug("Logo: width %d  height %d  colors %d  cmap %d\n",
		BMP_LOGO_WIDTH, BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT, BMP_LOGO_COLORS,
		ARRAY_SIZE(bmp_logo_palette));

	bmap = &bmp_logo_bitmap[0];
#ifdef CONFIG_RK_FB
	fb = (uchar *)(lcd_base);
	if(!rk_bitmap_from_resource((unsigned short*)fb))
		return;
#else
	fb   = (uchar *)(lcd_base + y * lcd_line_length + x * bpix / 8);
#endif

#ifdef CONFIG_RK_FB
{
#if (defined CONFIG_COMPRESS_LOGO_RLE8) || (defined CONFIG_COMPRESS_LOGO_RLE16)
	unsigned n, index;
	index = 0;
	for(i=0; i<(sizeof(bmp_logo_rle)/sizeof(bmp_logo_rle[0]) - 1);)
	{
		n = bmp_logo_rle[i++];
		memset(bmap + index, (uint8_t)bmp_logo_rle[i++], n);
		index += n;
	}
#endif
}
#endif /* rockchip fb */

	if (bpix < 12) {
		/* Leave room for default color map
		 * default case: generic system with no cmap (most likely 16bpp)
		 * cmap was set to the source palette, so no change is done.
		 * This avoids even more ifdefs in the next stanza
		 */
#if defined(CONFIG_MPC823)
		cmap = (ushort *) &(cp->lcd_cmap[BMP_LOGO_OFFSET * sizeof(ushort)]);
#elif defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD)
		cmap = (uint *)configuration_get_cmap();
#else
		cmap = configuration_get_cmap();
#endif

		WATCHDOG_RESET();

		/* Set color map */
		for (i = 0; i < ARRAY_SIZE(bmp_logo_palette); ++i) {
			ushort colreg = bmp_logo_palette[i];
#ifdef CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD
			uint lut_entry;
#ifdef CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD_BGR555
			lut_entry = ((colreg & 0x000F) << 11) |
					((colreg & 0x00F0) <<  2) |
					((colreg & 0x0F00) >>  7);
#else /* CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD_RGB565 */
			lut_entry = ((colreg & 0x000F) << 1) |
					((colreg & 0x00F0) << 3) |
					((colreg & 0x0F00) << 4);
#endif
			*(cmap + BMP_LOGO_OFFSET) = lut_entry;
			cmap++;
#else /* !CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD */
			*cmap++ = colreg;
#endif /* CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD */
		}

		WATCHDOG_RESET();

#ifdef CONFIG_RK_FB
		memcpy(fb, bmap, BMP_LOGO_WIDTH*BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT);
#else
		for (i = 0; i < BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT; ++i) {
			memcpy(fb, bmap, BMP_LOGO_WIDTH);
			bmap += BMP_LOGO_WIDTH;
			fb += panel_info.vl_col;
		}
#endif
	}
	else { /* true color mode */
		u16 col16;
		fb16 = (ushort *)fb;
		for (i = 0; i < BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT; ++i) {
			for (j = 0; j < BMP_LOGO_WIDTH; j++) {
				col16 = bmp_logo_palette[(bmap[j]-16)];
				fb16[j] =
					((col16 & 0x000F) << 1) |
					((col16 & 0x00F0) << 3) |
					((col16 & 0x0F00) << 4);
				}
			bmap += BMP_LOGO_WIDTH;
#ifdef CONFIG_RK_FB
			fb16 += BMP_LOGO_WIDTH;
#else
			fb16 += panel_info.vl_col;
#endif
		}
	}

	WATCHDOG_RESET();
#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
	{
		struct fb_dsp_info fb_info;
		fb_info.xpos = x;
		fb_info.ypos = y;
		fb_info.xact = BMP_LOGO_WIDTH;
		fb_info.yact = BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT;
		fb_info.xsize = fb_info.xact;
		fb_info.ysize = fb_info.yact;
		fb_info.xvir = fb_info.xact;
		fb_info.layer_id = WIN0;
		fb_info.format = RGB565;
		fb_info.yaddr = (u32)(unsigned long)lcd_base;
		lcd_pandispaly(&fb_info);
	}
#endif

	lcd_sync();
}
#else
static inline void bitmap_plot(int x, int y) {}
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_LOGO */

/*----------------------------------------------------------------------*/
#if defined(CONFIG_CMD_BMP) || defined(CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN)
/*
 * Display the BMP file located at address bmp_image.
 * Only uncompressed.
 */

#ifdef CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN_ALIGN
#define BMP_ALIGN_CENTER	0x7FFF

static void splash_align_axis(int *axis, unsigned long panel_size,
					unsigned long picture_size)
{
	unsigned long panel_picture_delta = panel_size - picture_size;
	unsigned long axis_alignment;

	if (*axis == BMP_ALIGN_CENTER)
		axis_alignment = panel_picture_delta / 2;
	else if (*axis < 0)
		axis_alignment = panel_picture_delta + *axis + 1;
	else
		return;

	*axis = max(0, axis_alignment);
}
#endif


#ifdef CONFIG_LCD_BMP_RLE8

#define BMP_RLE8_ESCAPE		0
#define BMP_RLE8_EOL		0
#define BMP_RLE8_EOBMP		1
#define BMP_RLE8_DELTA		2

static void draw_unencoded_bitmap(ushort **fbp, uchar *bmap, ushort *cmap,
				  int cnt)
{
	while (cnt > 0) {
		*(*fbp)++ = cmap[*bmap++];
		cnt--;
	}
}

static void draw_encoded_bitmap(ushort **fbp, ushort c, int cnt)
{
	ushort *fb = *fbp;
	int cnt_8copy = cnt >> 3;

	cnt -= cnt_8copy << 3;
	while (cnt_8copy > 0) {
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		*fb++ = c;
		cnt_8copy--;
	}
	while (cnt > 0) {
		*fb++ = c;
		cnt--;
	}
	*fbp = fb;
}

/*
 * Do not call this function directly, must be called from lcd_display_bitmap.
 */
static void lcd_display_rle8_bitmap(bmp_image_t *bmp, ushort *cmap, uchar *fb,
				    int x_off, int y_off)
{
	uchar *bmap;
	ulong width, height;
	ulong cnt, runlen;
	int x, y;
	int decode = 1;

	width = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.width);
	height = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.height);
	bmap = (uchar *)bmp + get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.data_offset);

	x = 0;
	y = height - 1;

	while (decode) {
		if (bmap[0] == BMP_RLE8_ESCAPE) {
			switch (bmap[1]) {
			case BMP_RLE8_EOL:
				/* end of line */
				bmap += 2;
				x = 0;
				y--;
				/* 16bpix, 2-byte per pixel, width should *2 */
				fb -= (width * 2 + lcd_line_length);
				break;
			case BMP_RLE8_EOBMP:
				/* end of bitmap */
				decode = 0;
				break;
			case BMP_RLE8_DELTA:
				/* delta run */
				x += bmap[2];
				y -= bmap[3];
				/* 16bpix, 2-byte per pixel, x should *2 */
				fb = (uchar *) (lcd_base + (y + y_off - 1)
					* lcd_line_length + (x + x_off) * 2);
				bmap += 4;
				break;
			default:
				/* unencoded run */
				runlen = bmap[1];
				bmap += 2;
				if (y < height) {
					if (x < width) {
						if (x + runlen > width)
							cnt = width - x;
						else
							cnt = runlen;
						draw_unencoded_bitmap(
							(ushort **)&fb,
							bmap, cmap, cnt);
					}
					x += runlen;
				}
				bmap += runlen;
				if (runlen & 1)
					bmap++;
			}
		} else {
			/* encoded run */
			if (y < height) {
				runlen = bmap[0];
				if (x < width) {
					/* aggregate the same code */
					while (bmap[0] == 0xff &&
					       bmap[2] != BMP_RLE8_ESCAPE &&
					       bmap[1] == bmap[3]) {
						runlen += bmap[2];
						bmap += 2;
					}
					if (x + runlen > width)
						cnt = width - x;
					else
						cnt = runlen;
					draw_encoded_bitmap((ushort **)&fb,
						cmap[bmap[1]], cnt);
				}
				x += runlen;
			}
			bmap += 2;
		}
	}
}
#endif

#if defined(CONFIG_MPC823) || defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
#define FB_PUT_BYTE(fb, from) *(fb)++ = (255 - *(from)++)
#else
#define FB_PUT_BYTE(fb, from) *(fb)++ = *(from)++
#endif

#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_16BPP)
#if defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD_BGR555)
static inline void fb_put_word(uchar **fb, uchar **from)
{
	*(*fb)++ = (((*from)[0] & 0x1f) << 2) | ((*from)[1] & 0x03);
	*(*fb)++ = ((*from)[0] & 0xe0) | (((*from)[1] & 0x7c) >> 2);
	*from += 2;
}
#else
static inline void fb_put_word(uchar **fb, uchar **from)
{
	*(*fb)++ = *(*from)++;
	*(*fb)++ = *(*from)++;
}
#endif
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_16BPP */

#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
int lcd_display_bitmap_center(ulong bmp_image)
{
    bmp_image_t *bmp=(bmp_image_t *)bmp_image;
    unsigned long width, height;

    if (!bmp || !(bmp->header.signature[0] == 'B' &&
        bmp->header.signature[1] == 'M')) {
        printf("Error: no valid bmp image at %lx, sign:%c %c\n",
				bmp_image, bmp->header.signature[0], bmp->header.signature[1]);                                       

        return 1;
    }

    width = le32_to_cpu(bmp->header.width);
    height = le32_to_cpu(bmp->header.height);

    return lcd_display_bitmap(bmp_image, (panel_info.vl_col - width)/2,
			(panel_info.vl_row - height)/2);
}
#endif

int lcd_display_bitmap(ulong bmp_image, int x, int y)
{
#if !defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
    //printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", get_unaligned_le16(&((bmp_image_t *)bmp_image)->header.bit_count), NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix));
#ifndef CONFIG_RK_FB
	ushort *cmap =   configuration_get_cmap();
#else
	ushort tmpmap[256];  /* sizeof(ushort) * 256 */
	ushort *cmap = tmpmap;
	struct fb_dsp_info fb_info;
	u8 format = RGB565;
#endif
#endif
	ushort *cmap_base = NULL;
	ushort i, j;
	uchar *fb;
	bmp_image_t *bmp = (bmp_image_t *)map_sysmem(bmp_image, 0);
	uchar *bmap;
	ushort padded_width;
	unsigned long width, height, byte_width;
	unsigned long pwidth = panel_info.vl_col;
	unsigned colors, bpix, bmp_bpix;
	if (!bmp || !(bmp->header.signature[0] == 'B' &&
		bmp->header.signature[1] == 'M')) {
		printf("Error: no valid bmp image at %lx, sign:%s\n", bmp_image, bmp->header.signature);

		return 1;
	}

	width = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.width);
	height = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.height);
	bmp_bpix = get_unaligned_le16(&bmp->header.bit_count);

	colors = 1 << bmp_bpix;

#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
	printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix);
	switch(bmp_bpix) {
	case 8:
	case 16:
		bpix = 16;
		format = RGB565;
		break;
	case 24:
		bpix = 32;
		format = ARGB888;
		break;
	case 32:
		bpix = 32;
		format = ARGB888;
		break;
	default:
		printf("Error: no support this bmp bpix%d\n",bmp_bpix);
		return -1;
	}
#else
	bpix = NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix);
	printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix, bpix);
	if (bpix != 1 && bpix != 8 && bpix != 16 && bpix != 32) {
		printf ("Error: %d bit/pixel mode, but BMP has %d bit/pixel\n",
			bpix, bmp_bpix);

		return 1;
	}

	/*
	 * We support displaying 8bpp BMPs on 16bpp LCDs
	 * and displaying 24bpp BMPs on 32bpp LCDs
	 * */
	if (bpix != bmp_bpix &&
	    !(bmp_bpix == 8 && bpix == 16) &&
	    !(bmp_bpix == 24 && bpix == 32)) {
		printf ("Error: %d bit/pixel mode, but BMP has %d bit/pixel\n",
			bpix, get_unaligned_le16(&bmp->header.bit_count));
		return 1;
	}
#endif

	debug("Display-bmp: %d x %d  with %d colors\n",
		(int)width, (int)height, (int)colors);


#if !defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
		// printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix, bpix);
	/* MCC200 LCD doesn't need CMAP, supports 1bpp b&w only */
	if (bmp_bpix == 8) {
		cmap_base = cmap;

		/* Set color map */
		for (i = 0; i < colors; ++i) {
			bmp_color_table_entry_t cte = bmp->color_table[i];
#if !defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD)
			ushort colreg =
				( ((cte.red)   << 8) & 0xf800) |
				( ((cte.green) << 3) & 0x07e0) |
				( ((cte.blue)  >> 3) & 0x001f) ;
			*cmap = colreg;
#if defined(CONFIG_MPC823)
			printf("xxxxxxxxBMP palette: %d: R %d G %d B %d -> 0x%04x\n", i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue, colreg);
			cmap--;
#else
			cmap++;
#endif
#else /* CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD */
			printf("BMP palette: %d: R %d G %d B %d\n", i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue);
			lcd_setcolreg(i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue);
#endif
		}
	}
#endif
	/*
	 *  BMP format for Monochrome assumes that the state of a
	 * pixel is described on a per Bit basis, not per Byte.
	 *  So, in case of Monochrome BMP we should align widths
	 * on a byte boundary and convert them from Bit to Byte
	 * units.
	 *  Probably, PXA250 and MPC823 process 1bpp BMP images in
	 * their own ways, so make the converting to be MCC200
	 * specific.
	 */
#if defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
	printf("MCC200: no support 1bpp bmp\n");
	if (bpix == 1) {
		width = ((width + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
		x     = ((x + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
		pwidth= ((pwidth + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
	}
#endif
	printf("Original width %d, padded width %d\n", (int)width, (int)padded_width);
	padded_width = (width & 0x3 ? (width & ~0x3) + 4 : width);

#ifdef CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN_ALIGN
	printf("Aligning the splash screen to %d x %d\n", pwidth, panel_info.vl_row);
	splash_align_axis(&x, pwidth, width);
	splash_align_axis(&y, panel_info.vl_row, height);
#endif /* CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN_ALIGN */

#ifndef CONFIG_PRODUCT_BOX
	if ((x + width) > pwidth)
		width = pwidth - x;
	if ((y + height) > panel_info.vl_row)
		height = panel_info.vl_row - y;
#endif
	printf("BMP: x %d y %d width %d height %d\n", x, y, width, height);
  	bmap = (uchar *)bmp + get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.data_offset);
#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
	/* rk charge mode, enable fb flip */
	if (lcd_flip) {
		printf("Flip the logo\n");
		if((unsigned long)lcd_base == gd->fb_base)
			lcd_base += width * height * bpix >> 3;
		else
			lcd_base = (void *)gd->fb_base;
	} else {
		printf("Normal display the logo\n");
		lcd_base = (void *)gd->fb_base;
	}
	lcd_base = (void *) ALIGN((ulong)lcd_base, CONFIG_LCD_ALIGNMENT);

	lcd_line_length = (width * bpix) / 8;
	fb = (uchar *) (lcd_base + ( height - 1) * lcd_line_length);
#else
	fb   = (uchar *)(lcd_base +
		(y + height - 1) * lcd_line_length + x * bpix / 8);
#endif

	switch (bmp_bpix) {
	case 1: /* pass through */
	case 8: {
#ifdef CONFIG_LCD_BMP_RLE8
		{
			printf("Displaying %dbpp RLE8 compressed BMP\n", bmp_bpix);
			u32 compression = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.compression);

			if (compression == BMP_BI_RLE8) {
				if (bpix != 16) {
					/* TODO implement render code for bpix != 16 */
					printf("Error: only support 16 bpix");
					return 1;
				}
				lcd_display_rle8_bitmap(bmp, cmap_base, fb, x, y);
				break;
			}
		}
#endif
		printf("Displaying %dbpp BMP\n", bmp_bpix);
		if (bpix != 16)
			byte_width = width;
		else
			byte_width = width * 2;

		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			WATCHDOG_RESET();
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
				if (bpix != 16) {
					FB_PUT_BYTE(fb, bmap);
				} else {
					*(uint16_t *)fb = cmap_base[*(bmap++)];
					fb += sizeof(uint16_t) / sizeof(*fb);
				}
			}
			bmap += (padded_width - width);
			fb -= byte_width + lcd_line_length;
		}
		break;
	}
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_16BPP)
	case 16:
		printf("Displaying 16bpp BMP\n");
		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			WATCHDOG_RESET();
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++)
				fb_put_word(&fb, &bmap);

			bmap += (padded_width - width) * 2;
			fb -= width * 2 + lcd_line_length;
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_16BPP */
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_24BPP)
	case 24:
		printf("Displaying 24bpp BMP\n");
		if (bpix == 32) {
			printf("Displaying 24bpp BMP on 32bpp LCD\n");
			ulong start_time = get_timer(0);
			for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
				for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = 0;
				}
				fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
			}
			printf("Frame display time: %lu ms\n", get_timer(start_time));
		} else if (bpix == 24) {
			for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
				for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				}
				fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
			}
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_24BMP */
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_32BPP)
	case 32:
		printf("Displaying 32bpp BMP\n");
		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
			}
			fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_32BPP */
	default:
		break;
	};
#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
#ifdef CONFIG_PRODUCT_BOX
	fb_info.xpos = 0;
	fb_info.ypos = 0;
	fb_info.xact = width;
	fb_info.yact = height;
	fb_info.xsize = panel_info.vl_col;
	fb_info.ysize = panel_info.vl_row;
#else
	fb_info.xpos = x;
	fb_info.ypos = y;
	fb_info.xact = width;
	fb_info.yact = height;
	fb_info.xsize = fb_info.xact;
	fb_info.ysize = fb_info.yact;
#endif
	
	fb_info.xvir = fb_info.xact;
	fb_info.layer_id = WIN0;
	fb_info.format = format;
	fb_info.yaddr = (u32)(unsigned long)lcd_base;
	// printf("fb_infoxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx");
	lcd_pandispaly(&fb_info);
#endif

	lcd_sync();
	return 0;
}




int lcd_prepare_bitmap(ulong bmp_image, int x, int y, ulong framebuffer)
{
	void *lcd_base = framebuffer;
#if !defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
    //printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", get_unaligned_le16(&((bmp_image_t *)bmp_image)->header.bit_count), NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix));
#ifndef CONFIG_RK_FB
	ushort *cmap =   configuration_get_cmap();
#else
	ushort tmpmap[256];  /* sizeof(ushort) * 256 */
	ushort *cmap = tmpmap;
	struct fb_dsp_info fb_info;
	u8 format = RGB565;
#endif
#endif
	ushort *cmap_base = NULL;
	ushort i, j;
	uchar *fb;
	bmp_image_t *bmp = (bmp_image_t *)map_sysmem(bmp_image, 0);
	uchar *bmap;
	ushort padded_width;
	unsigned long width, height, byte_width;
	unsigned long pwidth = panel_info.vl_col;
	unsigned colors, bpix, bmp_bpix;
	if (!bmp || !(bmp->header.signature[0] == 'B' &&
		bmp->header.signature[1] == 'M')) {
		printf("Error: no valid bmp image at %lx, sign:%s\n", bmp_image, bmp->header.signature);

		return 1;
	}

	width = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.width);
	height = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.height);
	bmp_bpix = get_unaligned_le16(&bmp->header.bit_count);

	colors = 1 << bmp_bpix;

#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
	printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix);
	switch(bmp_bpix) {
	case 8:
	case 16:
		bpix = 16;
		format = RGB565;
		break;
	case 24:
		bpix = 32;
		format = ARGB888;
		break;
	case 32:
		bpix = 32;
		format = ARGB888;
		break;
	default:
		printf("Error: no support this bmp bpix%d\n",bmp_bpix);
		return -1;
	}
#else
	bpix = NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix);
	printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix, bpix);
	if (bpix != 1 && bpix != 8 && bpix != 16 && bpix != 32) {
		printf ("Error: %d bit/pixel mode, but BMP has %d bit/pixel\n",
			bpix, bmp_bpix);

		return 1;
	}

	/*
	 * We support displaying 8bpp BMPs on 16bpp LCDs
	 * and displaying 24bpp BMPs on 32bpp LCDs
	 * */
	if (bpix != bmp_bpix &&
	    !(bmp_bpix == 8 && bpix == 16) &&
	    !(bmp_bpix == 24 && bpix == 32)) {
		printf ("Error: %d bit/pixel mode, but BMP has %d bit/pixel\n",
			bpix, get_unaligned_le16(&bmp->header.bit_count));
		return 1;
	}
#endif

	debug("Display-bmp: %d x %d  with %d colors\n",
		(int)width, (int)height, (int)colors);


#if !defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
		// printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", bmp_bpix, bpix);
	/* MCC200 LCD doesn't need CMAP, supports 1bpp b&w only */
	if (bmp_bpix == 8) {
		cmap_base = cmap;

		/* Set color map */
		for (i = 0; i < colors; ++i) {
			bmp_color_table_entry_t cte = bmp->color_table[i];
#if !defined(CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD)
			ushort colreg =
				( ((cte.red)   << 8) & 0xf800) |
				( ((cte.green) << 3) & 0x07e0) |
				( ((cte.blue)  >> 3) & 0x001f) ;
			*cmap = colreg;
#if defined(CONFIG_MPC823)
			printf("xxxxxxxxBMP palette: %d: R %d G %d B %d -> 0x%04x\n", i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue, colreg);
			cmap--;
#else
			cmap++;
#endif
#else /* CONFIG_ATMEL_LCD */
			printf("BMP palette: %d: R %d G %d B %d\n", i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue);
			lcd_setcolreg(i, cte.red, cte.green, cte.blue);
#endif
		}
	}
#endif
	/*
	 *  BMP format for Monochrome assumes that the state of a
	 * pixel is described on a per Bit basis, not per Byte.
	 *  So, in case of Monochrome BMP we should align widths
	 * on a byte boundary and convert them from Bit to Byte
	 * units.
	 *  Probably, PXA250 and MPC823 process 1bpp BMP images in
	 * their own ways, so make the converting to be MCC200
	 * specific.
	 */
#if defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
	printf("MCC200: no support 1bpp bmp\n");
	if (bpix == 1) {
		width = ((width + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
		x     = ((x + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
		pwidth= ((pwidth + 7) & ~7) >> 3;
	}
#endif
	printf("Original width %d, padded width %d\n", (int)width, (int)padded_width);
	padded_width = (width & 0x3 ? (width & ~0x3) + 4 : width);

#ifdef CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN_ALIGN
	printf("Aligning the splash screen to %d x %d\n", pwidth, panel_info.vl_row);
	splash_align_axis(&x, pwidth, width);
	splash_align_axis(&y, panel_info.vl_row, height);
#endif /* CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN_ALIGN */

#ifndef CONFIG_PRODUCT_BOX
	if ((x + width) > pwidth)
		width = pwidth - x;
	if ((y + height) > panel_info.vl_row)
		height = panel_info.vl_row - y;
#endif
	printf("BMP: x %d y %d width %d height %d\n", x, y, width, height);
  	bmap = (uchar *)bmp + get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.data_offset);
#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)

	printf("Normal display the logo\n");
	lcd_base = (void *)framebuffer;

	lcd_base = (void *) ALIGN((ulong)lcd_base, CONFIG_LCD_ALIGNMENT);

	lcd_line_length = (width * bpix) / 8;
	fb = (uchar *) (lcd_base + ( height - 1) * lcd_line_length);
#else
	fb   = (uchar *)(lcd_base +
		(y + height - 1) * lcd_line_length + x * bpix / 8);
#endif

	switch (bmp_bpix) {
	case 1: /* pass through */
	case 8: {
#ifdef CONFIG_LCD_BMP_RLE8
		{
			printf("Displaying %dbpp RLE8 compressed BMP\n", bmp_bpix);
			u32 compression = get_unaligned_le32(&bmp->header.compression);

			if (compression == BMP_BI_RLE8) {
				if (bpix != 16) {
					/* TODO implement render code for bpix != 16 */
					printf("Error: only support 16 bpix");
					return 1;
				}
				lcd_display_rle8_bitmap(bmp, cmap_base, fb, x, y);
				break;
			}
		}
#endif
		printf("Displaying %dbpp BMP\n", bmp_bpix);
		if (bpix != 16)
			byte_width = width;
		else
			byte_width = width * 2;

		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			WATCHDOG_RESET();
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
				if (bpix != 16) {
					FB_PUT_BYTE(fb, bmap);
				} else {
					*(uint16_t *)fb = cmap_base[*(bmap++)];
					fb += sizeof(uint16_t) / sizeof(*fb);
				}
			}
			bmap += (padded_width - width);
			fb -= byte_width + lcd_line_length;
		}
		break;
	}
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_16BPP)
	case 16:
		printf("Displaying 16bpp BMP\n");
		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			WATCHDOG_RESET();
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++)
				fb_put_word(&fb, &bmap);

			bmap += (padded_width - width) * 2;
			fb -= width * 2 + lcd_line_length;
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_16BPP */
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_24BPP)
	case 24:
		printf("Displaying 24bpp BMP\n");
		if (bpix == 32) {
			printf("Displaying 24bpp BMP on 32bpp LCD\n");
			ulong start_time = get_timer(0);
			for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
				for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = 0;
				}
				fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
			}
			printf("Frame display time: %lu ms\n", get_timer(start_time));
		} else if (bpix == 24) {
			for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
				for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
					*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				}
				fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
			}
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_24BMP */
#if defined(CONFIG_BMP_32BPP)
	case 32:
		printf("Displaying 32bpp BMP\n");
		for (i = 0; i < height; ++i) {
			for (j = 0; j < width; j++) {
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
				*(fb++) = *(bmap++);
			}
			fb -= lcd_line_length + width * (bpix / 8);
		}
		break;
#endif /* CONFIG_BMP_32BPP */
	default:
		break;
	};
	gx = x;
	gy = y;
	gwidth = width;
	gheight = height;
	g_format = format;
	return 0;
}


int display_framebuffer(uint32_t addr)
{
	int x = gx;
	int y = gy;
	int width = gwidth;
	int height = gheight;
	int format = g_format;
	void *lcd_base = (void *)addr;
#if !defined(CONFIG_MCC200)
    //printf("BMP: %d bit/pixel, LCD: %d bit/pixel\n", get_unaligned_le16(&((bmp_image_t *)bmp_image)->header.bit_count), NBITS(panel_info.vl_bpix));
#ifndef CONFIG_RK_FB
#else
	struct fb_dsp_info fb_info;
#endif
#endif
#if defined(CONFIG_RK_FB)
#ifdef CONFIG_PRODUCT_BOX
	fb_info.xpos = 0;
	fb_info.ypos = 0;
	fb_info.xact = width;
	fb_info.yact = height;
	fb_info.xsize = panel_info.vl_col;
	fb_info.ysize = panel_info.vl_row;
#else
	fb_info.xpos = x;
	fb_info.ypos = y;
	fb_info.xact = width;
	fb_info.yact = height;
	fb_info.xsize = fb_info.xact;
	fb_info.ysize = fb_info.yact;
#endif
	
	fb_info.xvir = fb_info.xact;
	fb_info.layer_id = WIN0;
	fb_info.format = format;
	fb_info.yaddr = (u32)(unsigned long)lcd_base;
	// printf("fb_infoxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx");
	lcd_pandispaly(&fb_info);
#endif

	lcd_sync();
	return 0;
}




#endif

static void *lcd_logo(void)
{
#ifdef CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN
	char *s;
	ulong addr;
	static int do_splash = 1;

	if (do_splash && (s = getenv("splashimage")) != NULL) {
		int x = 0, y = 0;
		do_splash = 0;

		if (splash_screen_prepare())
			return (void *)lcd_base;

		addr = simple_strtoul (s, NULL, 16);

		splash_get_pos(&x, &y);

		if (bmp_display(addr, x, y) == 0)
			return (void *)lcd_base;
	}
#endif /* CONFIG_SPLASH_SCREEN */

#ifndef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
	bitmap_plot(0, 0);
#else
	bitmap_plot((panel_info.vl_col - BMP_LOGO_WIDTH)/2, (panel_info.vl_row - BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT)/2);
#endif

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
#ifdef CONFIG_LCD_INFO
	console_col = LCD_INFO_X / VIDEO_FONT_WIDTH;
	console_row = LCD_INFO_Y / VIDEO_FONT_HEIGHT;
	lcd_show_board_info();
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_INFO */
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

#if defined(CONFIG_LCD_LOGO) && !defined(CONFIG_LCD_INFO_BELOW_LOGO)
	return (void *)((ulong)lcd_base + BMP_LOGO_HEIGHT * lcd_line_length);
#else
	return (void *)lcd_base;
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_LOGO && !defined(CONFIG_LCD_INFO_BELOW_LOGO) */
}

#ifdef CONFIG_SPLASHIMAGE_GUARD
static int on_splashimage(const char *name, const char *value, enum env_op op,
	int flags)
{
	ulong addr;
	int aligned;

	if (op == env_op_delete)
		return 0;

	addr = simple_strtoul(value, NULL, 16);
	/* See README.displaying-bmps */
	aligned = (addr % 4 == 2);
	if (!aligned) {
		printf("Invalid splashimage value. Value must be 16 bit aligned, but not 32 bit aligned\n");
		return -1;
	}

	return 0;
}

U_BOOT_ENV_CALLBACK(splashimage, on_splashimage);
#endif

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
void lcd_position_cursor(unsigned col, unsigned row)
{
	console_col = min(col, CONSOLE_COLS - 1);
	console_row = min(row, CONSOLE_ROWS - 1);
}
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

	return panel_info.vl_col;
}

int lcd_get_pixel_height(void)
{
	return panel_info.vl_row;
}

#ifndef CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE
int lcd_get_screen_rows(void)
{
	return CONSOLE_ROWS;
}

int lcd_get_screen_columns(void)
{
	return CONSOLE_COLS;
}
#endif /* CONFIG_LCD_CONSOLE_DISABLE */

#if defined(CONFIG_LCD_DT_SIMPLEFB)
static int lcd_dt_simplefb_configure_node(void *blob, int off)
{
#if LCD_BPP == LCD_COLOR16
	return fdt_setup_simplefb_node(blob, off, gd->fb_base,
				       panel_info.vl_col, panel_info.vl_row,
				       panel_info.vl_col * 2, "r5g6b5");
#else
	return -1;
#endif
}

int lcd_dt_simplefb_add_node(void *blob)
{
	static const char compat[] = "simple-framebuffer";
	static const char disabled[] = "disabled";
	int off, ret;

	off = fdt_add_subnode(blob, 0, "framebuffer");
	if (off < 0)
		return -1;

	ret = fdt_setprop(blob, off, "status", disabled, sizeof(disabled));
	if (ret < 0)
		return -1;

	ret = fdt_setprop(blob, off, "compatible", compat, sizeof(compat));
	if (ret < 0)
		return -1;

	return lcd_dt_simplefb_configure_node(blob, off);
}

int lcd_dt_simplefb_enable_existing_node(void *blob)
{
	int off;

	off = fdt_node_offset_by_compatible(blob, -1, "simple-framebuffer");
	if (off < 0)
		return -1;

	return lcd_dt_simplefb_configure_node(blob, off);
}
#endif
