DECLARE_GLOBAL_DATA_PTR;


#if defined(CONFIG_LCD) && defined(CONFIG_KERNEL_LOGO)
static int g_rk_fb_size = -1;

#endif





#ifdef CONFIG_ROCKCHIP
int lcd_prepare_bitmap_center(ulong bmp_image, ulong framebuffer)
{
    bmp_image_t *bmp=(bmp_image_t *)bmp_image;
    unsigned long width, height;

    if (!bmp || !(bmp->header.signature[0] == 'B' &&
        bmp->header.signature[1] == 'M')) {
        printf("Error: no valid bmp image at %lx, sign:%c %c\n",
				bmp_image, bmp->header.signature[0], bmp->header.signature[1]);                                       

        return 1;
    }

    width = le32_to_cpu(bmp->header.width);
    height = le32_to_cpu(bmp->header.height);

    return lcd_prepare_bitmap(bmp_image, (panel_info.vl_col - width)/2,
			(panel_info.vl_row - height)/2, framebuffer);
}
#endif



bool load_resource_image(const char* image_path, char* load_addr, int* size) {
	if(image_path) printf("load_resource_image: image_path = %s\n", image_path);
	bool ret = false;
#ifdef CONFIG_LCD
	resource_content image;
	memset(&image, 0, sizeof(image));
	snprintf(image.path, sizeof(image.path), "%s", image_path);

	if (get_content(0, &image)) {
		debug("%s:show logo from resource or boot partition\n", __func__);
		debug("image content offset: %d, size: %d\n", image.content_offset, image.content_size);
		int blocks = (image.content_size + BLOCK_SIZE - 1) / BLOCK_SIZE;
		*size = image.content_size;
		if (image.content_size > CONFIG_RK_BOOT_BUFFER_SIZE) {
			FBTERR("Failed to bmp image too large, %d\n",
					image.content_size);
			return false;
		}

		// image.load_addr = (void *)gd->arch.rk_boot_buf_addr;
		if (!load_content_data(&image, 0, load_addr, blocks)) {
			return false;
		}

		ret = true;
	} else {
		FBTERR("Failed to load image:%s\n", image_path);
	}

#endif
	return ret;
}



static int rk_load_slide(const char* file_path)
{
	if (!file_path) file_path = "logo.bmp";
	show_resource_image(file_path);
	return 1;
}
static int rk_play_slideshow(int delay_ms)
{
	if (!delay_ms) delay_ms = 100000; // Default to 100 ms
	const int FRAME_COUNT = 4;
	const char* file_path[4] = {"frame1.bmp", "frame2.bmp", "frame3.bmp", "frame4.bmp"};
	char* frame_buffers[FRAME_COUNT];
	char* image_addr = (char *)gd->arch.rk_boot_buf_addr;
	int i = 0;
	bool run = true;
	int size = 0;
	for (i = 0; i < FRAME_COUNT; i++) {
		if (!load_resource_image(file_path[i], image_addr + i * size, &size)) {
			FBTERR("Failed to load slide %s\n", file_path[i]);
			return -1;
		}
		frame_buffers[i] = image_addr + (FRAME_COUNT + i) * size / 3 * 4;
		lcd_prepare_bitmap_center((ulong)(image_addr + i * size), (ulong)(frame_buffers[i]));
	}
	while (run)
	{
		/* code */
		for (i = 0; i < FRAME_COUNT; i++) {
			FBTDBG("Try to show:%s\n", image_path);
			display_framebuffer((uint32_t)(unsigned long)frame_buffers[i]);
			if (tstc()) {	/* we got a key press	*/
# ifdef CONFIG_MENUKEY
				char menukey = getc();
# else
				(void) getc();  /* consume input	*/
# endif
				run = false;
				break;
			}
			udelay(delay_ms * 1000); 
		}
	}
	return 1;
}

/* slideshow [ mode ] */
int do_slideshow(cmd_tbl_t *cmdtp, int flag, int argc, char * const argv[])
{
	if (argc < 2) {
		printf("invalid argument.\n");
		printf("use slideshow [mode] [delay_ms].\n");
		printf("mode: 1 - play slideshow\n");
		printf("mode: 2 - show animation\n");
		return -1;
	}
	const char* mode = argv[1];
	int delay_ms = 100; // Default to 100 ms
	if (argc > 2) {
		delay_ms = simple_strtoul(argv[2], NULL, 10);
	}
	printf("play slideshow with mode %s and delay %d ms\n", mode, delay_ms);
	if(strcmp(mode, "0") == 0) {
		rk_load_slide("bg0.bmp");
	} else if(strcmp(mode, "1") == 0) {
		rk_load_slide("bg1.bmp");
	} else if(strcmp(mode, "2") == 0) {
		rk_play_slideshow(delay_ms);
	} else {
		printf("invalid mode.\n");
		return -1;
	}
	return 0;
}

U_BOOT_CMD(
		slideshow,	3,	1,	do_slideshow,
		"play slideshow\n",
#ifdef DEBUG
		"\n"
#else
		"\n"
#endif
		);

-------------------------------------------------

kernel hdmi驱动

在 RK30 以后（RK30XX、RK292X、RK31XX）的平台上，fb 驱动被分为：
	fb 框架相关的部分
	LCDC 控制器相关的部分
	LCD 屏幕相关的部分
	LCD 电源操作相关的板级配置部分

2.1 fb 框架相关的代码
	drivers/video/fbmem.c          其中 fbmem.c 为 linux 内核原生代码，他向上提供和用户空间交互的接口（open、read、write、ioctl 等），向下联系平台相关的 fb 驱动 rk_fb.c。
	drivers/video/rockchip/rk_fb.c
	drivers/video/rockchip/rkfb_sysfs.c
	include/linux/rk_fb.h
	include/linux/rk_screen.h
 这部分代码实现和 fb 相关的框架，不涉及具体的硬件操作

 2.2 LCDC 相关的代码
	drivers/video/rockchip/lcdc/rkxxx_lcdc.c：
	drivers/video/rockchip/lcdc/rk30_lcdc.c
	drivers/video/rockchip/lcdc/rk3066b_lcdc.c
	drivers/video/rockchip/lcdc/rk2928_lcdc.c
	drivers/video/rockchip/lcdc/rk3188_lcdc.c
 这部分代码和具体的 LCDC 控制器相关，不同的 LCDC 控制器对应的代码不同。


 2.3 LCD 屏幕配置相关代码
	drivers/video/rockchip/screen/rk_screen.c
	drivers/video/rockchip/screeen/lcd_xxx.c
rk_screen.c 是屏幕配置文件的共用代码，主要实现如下接口：
set_scaler_info:使用主控的一个 LCDC+RK610 或者 RK616 的 scaler 实现双显的配置接口，只有这种双显模式下才会用到。
set_lcd_info：屏幕参数配置接口，所有的屏幕都会用到
get_fb_size: 根据屏幕的分辨率计算需要分配多大的 fb 空间，对于三 buffer，计算公式为 X*Y*4*3,双 buffer 计算公式为 X*Y*4*2，目前我们都使用三 buffer。
建议每个项目相关的人员都要看下 rk_screen.c 中相关接口的实现，以方便开发中遇到的 debug 问题。
lcd_xxx.c 是屏幕参数配置文件，而且必须以 lcd_xxx.c（即以 lcd_开头）的格式命名。在编译的时候经过 Makefile 的特殊处理，lcd_xxx.c 中的内容会被拷贝到生
成的 lcd.h 文件中，rk_screen.c 会包含 lcd.h 这个头文件，然后引用对应屏幕配置文件中定义的相关参数去进行初始化。

5 基于 rk fb 驱动的应用开发
首先 rk fb 是遵循 linux frame buffer 驱动扩展的 fb 驱动，因此基于 rk fb 的应用开发基本和标准的 linux frame buffer 应用开发一致。
RK 系列主控的 LCDC 在内部是分层的，每一层叫做 win，每一层可以在屏幕上任意位置显示支持范围内任意大小的图像，并且各层可以通过 alpha blending 或者 color key 实现 overlay 合成输出。
其中 RK3066 的 LCDC 有三层，win0、win1、win2，win0、win1 支持 RGB 和 YUV 格式、win2 只支持 YUV 格式。RK292X、RK3168、RK3188 的 LCDC 有两层，win0 支持 RGB 和 YUV 格式，win1 只支持 RGB 格式。

在 rk fb 中，每一层 win 对应一个 fb 设备，它们在 linux 系统中对应的设备节点为/dev/graphics/fbx,其中 win 和 fb 的对应关系是可以通过程序设置的，以 RK3066为例：
 /dev/graphics/fb0-----win1
 /dev/graphics/fb1-----win0
 /dev/graphics/fb2-----win2
 具体的对应关系可以通过 cat sys/class/graphics/fb0/map 节点查询： 

 5.2相关系统调用：
 Fb 设备作为一个标准的字符设备，需要通过相关的系统调用对其进行操作，主要是 open、close、mmap、以及相关的 ioctl 调用，可以以 android sdk 中的 hal 层代码作为参考：
 androidsrc/hardware/rk29/libgralloc_ump/framebuffer_device.cpp
（1）open
 在使用某个 fb 设备之前必须先 open：
 Fd = open(/dev/graphics/fbx, O_RDWR, 0);
（2）mmap
该调用用于将在内核中分配的 fb 地址映射到用户空间，以方便应用进行读写。
void* vaddr = mmap(0, fbSize, PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE, MAP_SHARED, fd, 0);
内核虚拟地址 (kernel virtual address),
用户空间
0x00000000
   |
   |  用户程序
   |
0x7fffffffffff
-------------------  用户 / 内核分界
0xffff800000000000
   |
   |  内核空间
   |  framebuffer
   |
0xffffffffffffffff


这是 操作系统安全模型。用户程序如果能访问内核地址：
可以改内核数据
可以破坏驱动
可以读内核隐私
所以 CPU 有权限级别：
x86：
Ring0  内核
Ring3  用户
ARM：
EL1 内核
EL0 用户
用户程序访问内核地址：
MMU 会直接拒绝

---------------------------
Linux framebuffer 参数如何决定“从显存的哪一块区域取数据去显示”

1. 显存（framebuffer）可能比屏幕大
2. xoffset / yoffset 决定当前显示窗口的位置

---

# 一、framebuffer 内存和屏幕不是一一对应的

很多人以为：

```
屏幕分辨率 = framebuffer大小
```

其实不是。

例如屏幕：

```
800 × 480
ARGB8888
```

一帧大小：

```
800 × 480 × 4 = 1.5MB
```

但驱动可能申请：

```
800 × 960 × 4
```

也就是：

```
2帧
```

内存结构：

```
framebuffer memory

+------------------+
| frame0 (800x480) |
+------------------+
| frame1 (800x480) |
+------------------+
```

这就是 **双缓冲**。

---

# 二、xres / yres 是什么

xres / yres 表示：

**当前屏幕实际显示区域大小**

例如：

```
xres = 800
yres = 480
```

表示：

```
屏幕可见区域
800 × 480
```

---

# 三、xres_virtual / yres_virtual

表示：

**framebuffer 内存的逻辑大小**

例如：

```
xres_virtual = 800
yres_virtual = 960
```

说明：

```
显存逻辑大小
800 × 960
```

内存布局：

```
0
│
│ frame0
│
480
│
│ frame1
│
960
```

---

# 四、stride（步长）是什么

stride 就是：

**一行在内存里的实际长度**

通常：

```
stride = xres_virtual × bytes_per_pixel
```

例如：

```
xres_virtual = 800
bpp = 4
```

那么：

```
stride = 3200 bytes
```

表示：

```
每一行占 3200 字节
```

---

# 五、xoffset / yoffset 是关键

这是 **显示窗口的位置**。

LCDC 并不是总从 framebuffer 的 **第 0 行** 显示。

而是：

```
从 (xoffset , yoffset) 开始显示
```

例如：

```
xoffset = 0
yoffset = 0
```

显示：

```
frame0
```

如果：

```
xoffset = 0
yoffset = 480
```

显示：

```
frame1
```

---

# 六、地址是怎么计算的

framebuffer 显示起始地址：

```
addr =
fb_base +
(yoffset * stride) +
(xoffset * bytes_per_pixel)
```

例如：

```
fb_base = 0x60000000
stride = 3200
bpp = 4
```

如果：

```
xoffset = 0
yoffset = 480
```

则：

```
addr = 0x60000000 + 480 × 3200
```

就是第二帧。

---

# 七、为什么需要这个机制

这是为了实现：

### 1 双缓冲（double buffer）

应用程序：

```
写 frame1
```

显示器：

```
显示 frame0
```

当写完：

```
yoffset = 480
```

显示切换。

效果：

```
不会闪屏
```

---

### 2 panning（滚屏）

例如 framebuffer：

```
2000 × 480
```

屏幕：

```
800 × 480
```

就可以：

```
xoffset 改变
```

实现：

```
横向滚动
```

类似：

```
大画布
```

---

# 八、一张完整示意图

假设：

```
屏幕
800 × 480
```

framebuffer：

```
800 × 960
```

内存：

```
fb_base
│
├───────────────
│ frame0
│ 800 × 480
│
├───────────────
│ frame1
│ 800 × 480
│
└───────────────
```

如果：

```
yoffset = 0
```

显示：

```
frame0
```

如果：

```
yoffset = 480
```

显示：

```
frame1
```

---

# 九、在代码里是这样切换的

应用程序：

```c
fb_var.yoffset = 480;

ioctl(fd, FBIOPAN_DISPLAY, &fb_var);
```

内核就会：

```
改变 LCDC 读取地址
```

于是：

```
frame1 → 显示
```

---

# 十、结合你现在研究的 RK3128

RK3128 的显示链路：

```
DDR framebuffer
       │
       │ (addr = base + offset)
       ▼
LCDC / VOP
       │
       ▼
HDMI controller
       │
       ▼
显示器
```

LCDC 每一帧都会从：

```
fb_base + offset
```

开始 DMA 读数据。

---

# 十一、很多资料没讲清的一点

`xres_virtual` **经常大于 xres**，原因是：

GPU / LCDC 常要求：

```
stride 16字节对齐
或
64字节对齐
```

例如：

```
屏幕 1366
```

实际：

```
stride = 1408
```

所以：

```
xres_virtual = 1408
```

---

如果你愿意，我可以再给你讲一个 **理解 framebuffer / LCDC 驱动最关键的一件事**：

**为什么很多 RK3128 / RK3288 的 framebuffer 地址必须 64 字节对齐，否则 HDMI 会花屏。**

这个其实是 **LCDC DMA burst 机制导致的**。
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

这段话其实是在说：**有些显示控制器（例如很多 SoC 的 LCDC / VOP / overlay layer）支持“图层位置、缩放、格式”等功能，但 Linux 原生 framebuffer API 没有标准字段来表达，所以有些厂商驱动会“借用” `fb_var_screen_info` 里未使用的成员来传这些参数。**

你看到的 **xpos、ypos、xsize、ysize、data_format** 本质上就是 **图层（layer / window）的显示属性**。

先建立一个正确的模型。

很多显示控制器不是只有一个 framebuffer，而是 **多层合成**：

```
UI layer
video layer
cursor layer
----------------
display mixer
----------------
HDMI/LCD
```

例如很多 Rockchip SoC 的 VOP 都支持 **window0 / window1 / overlay**。

每个 layer 都可以设置：

* 从 framebuffer 哪个区域取数据
* 在屏幕哪个位置显示
* 显示多大
* 数据格式是什么

下面逐个解释。

---

# 1 xpos / ypos

**含义：图层在屏幕上的显示位置**

单位：像素。

```
(xpos , ypos)
```

表示 **图层左上角在屏幕上的坐标**。

示例：

屏幕：

```
1280 × 720
```

如果

```
xpos = 0
ypos = 0
```

图像从屏幕左上角开始显示。

```
+-----------------------+
| IMAGE                 |
|                       |
|                       |
+-----------------------+
```

如果：

```
xpos = 200
ypos = 100
```

效果：

```
+-----------------------+
|                       |
|      IMAGE            |
|                       |
+-----------------------+
```

所以：

```
xpos → X方向偏移
ypos → Y方向偏移
```

---

# 2 xsize / ysize

**含义：图层在屏幕上显示的大小**

单位：像素。

注意：

```
xsize / ysize ≠ framebuffer原始大小
```

因为很多显示控制器支持 **缩放（scaler）**。

例如 framebuffer：

```
640 × 360
```

如果设置：

```
xsize = 1280
ysize = 720
```

硬件会：

```
640×360 → scale → 1280×720
```

这就是 **硬件缩放**。

示意：

```
source buffer
640×360

        scaler

display
1280×720
```

如果：

```
xsize = 320
ysize = 180
```

就会 **缩小显示**。

---

# 3 data_format

**含义：framebuffer数据格式**

因为 framebuffer 里的像素可能有很多格式：

常见格式：

| 格式       | 每像素   |
| -------- | ----- |
| RGB565   | 16bit |
| RGB888   | 24bit |
| ARGB8888 | 32bit |
| YUV420   | 视频    |

例如：

```
data_format = RGB565
```

表示：

```
pixel layout

rrrrr gggggg bbbbb
```

如果：

```
data_format = ARGB8888
```

表示：

```
AAAA RRRR GGGG BBBB
```

显示控制器必须知道格式，否则会解析错像素。

例如：

```
0xF800
```

在 RGB565 是：

```
红色
```

但如果当 ARGB8888 解析就会完全错。

---

# 4 为什么 fb API 没有这些字段

Linux 原生 framebuffer API 设计很早（90年代），目标只是：

```
一个 framebuffer
全屏显示
```

核心结构：

fb_var_screen_info

只包含：

```
xres
yres
xoffset
yoffset
bits_per_pixel
```

它假设：

```
framebuffer = 整个屏幕
```

而现代 SoC：

```
多layer
缩放
alpha
blending
```

所以很多厂商驱动会：

```
hack fb_var_screen_info
```

利用未用字段传参数。

---

# 5 一张完整关系图

假设 framebuffer：

```
source buffer
640 × 360
```

驱动设置：

```
xpos  = 100
ypos  = 50

xsize = 800
ysize = 450
```

显示结果：

```
screen 1280×720

+--------------------------------+
|                                |
|      +------------------+      |
|      | scaled image     |      |
|      | 800×450          |      |
|      +------------------+      |
|                                |
+--------------------------------+
```

---

# 6 和 xoffset / yoffset 的区别

很多人容易混淆。

| 参数              | 含义                    |
| --------------- | --------------------- |
| xoffset/yoffset | 从 framebuffer 哪个位置取数据 |
| xpos/ypos       | 显示在屏幕的哪个位置            |
| xsize/ysize     | 在屏幕上显示多大              |

示例：

framebuffer：

```
1920 × 1080
```

但只取一部分：

```
xoffset = 100
yoffset = 50
```

然后：

```
xpos = 200
ypos = 200
```

表示：

```
从buffer中裁剪一块
再显示到屏幕某位置
```

---

# 7 在 RK 系列芯片里

Rockchip 的 VOP window 通常支持：

```
source:
src_w
src_h

display:
dst_w
dst_h
dst_x
dst_y
```

其实就对应：

```
src_w/h  → framebuffer大小
dst_w/h  → xsize/ysize
dst_x/y  → xpos/ypos
```

---

# 8 你以后会遇到的更高级参数

很多显示控制器还有：

```
alpha
z-order
color key
rotation
```

所以现代 Linux 已经不用 framebuffer 体系了，而用：

```
DRM / KMS
```

相关结构：

Direct Rendering Manager

DRM 可以正式描述：

```
plane
crtc
overlay
scaler
```

---

如果你继续深入 **RK3128 HDMI / VOP**，我可以给你画一张 **Rockchip 显示 pipeline 的真实结构图**，把：

```
VOP
overlay
scaler
HDMI
framebuffer
```

之间的关系一次讲清楚。这个结构理解了，看驱动代码会容易很多。
---------------------------------------------------------------

User system call ---->fbmem.c ----->rk_fb.c ---->rkxxx_lcdc.c

Open---->fb_open(fbmem.c)--->rk_fb_open(rk_fb.c)--->rkxxx_lcdc_open(rkxxx_lcdc.c)
Ioctl--->fb_ioctl(fbmem.c)--->do_fb_ioctl(fbmem.c)-->rk_fb_ioctl(rk_fb.c)--->rkxxx_lcdc_ioctl(rkxxx_lcdc.c)


echo x > sys/module/rk30_lcdc/parameters/dbg_thresd
 该打印是分级别的，x=0 不打印，x=1 打印部分关键信息，x=2 打印更多信息

 同时可以 cat 如下节点获取更加详细的配置显示信息
cat sys/class/graphics/fb0/disp_info 



c. 硬件加速
支持多种硬件加速：

RGA（图形加速器）：图像旋转、缩放

IPP（图像后处理器）：图像处理

ION 内存管理：高效的内存分配

echo "switching root..."
mount --move /dev /mnt/dev 
mount --move /proc /mnt/proc 
mount --move /sys /mnt/sys
exec switch_root /mnt /sbin/init



//initramfs

#!/bin/sh
mount -t proc proc /proc
mount -t sysfs sysfs /sys
mount -t devtmpfs devtmpfs /dev
mkdir -p /dev/input
exec /bin/sh

1.编译busybox
find ~/rootfs -type l -delete
export PATH=$HOME/gcc-linaro-arm-linux-gnueabi-2012.03-20120326_linux/bin:$PATH
make ARCH=arm CROSS_COMPILE=arm-linux-gnueabi- -j8 CONFIG_PREFIX=~/rootfs install
2.创建目录结构和软连接
rootfs/
├── bin/busybox
├── bin/sh -> busybox
├── bin/ls -> busybox
├── sbin/init -> busybox
├── sbin/mdev -> busybox
├── etc/inittab
├── etc/init.d/rcS
├── dev/
├── proc/
├── sys/
└── root/flappyshark

inittab内容：
::sysinit:/etc/init.d/rcS
::respawn:/bin/sh
或者：
::respawn:/root/flappyshark

chmod +x etc/init.d/rcS
rcS内容：
#!/bin/sh

mount -t proc none /proc
mount -t sysfs none /sys
mount -t devtmpfs none /dev

echo /sbin/mdev > /proc/sys/kernel/hotplug
mdev -s

echo "System ready"
3.创建 ext4 镜像文件，64M，现在64M就够用，太大也行，就是下载太慢
dd if=/dev/zero of=rootfs.img bs=1M count=64

4.格式化成 ext4
mkfs.ext4 rootfs.img

5.挂载镜像，也可以用mnt,wsl中mnt已经挂载成windows目录了
mkdir mnt_rootfs
sudo mount -o loop rootfs.img mnt_rootfs

6.拷贝 rootfs 文件内容,一定要-a参数
sudo cp -a rootfs/* mnt_rootfs/

7.处理权限
sudo chown -R root:root mnt_rootfs/

8.卸载
sudo umount mnt_rootfs

9.烧写镜像
烧写的时候要修改对应的分区名称和地址，名称不区分大小写
linuxroot

10.复制到windows目录，准备烧录
cp rootfs.img /mnt/f/rk3128/


内存映射定义：
MMU 是 CPU 内部的硬件单元（SoC 里，属于 CPU 核的一部分）
RK3128（ARM Cortex-A7）里：
CPU Core
 ├─ ALU
 ├─ Cache（L1）
 ├─ TLB
 └─ MMU   ← 就在这里
 是 CPU流水线的一部分。
页表在 DDR（普通内存）里
MMU 内部并不存完整页表，它只有：
1. TTBR（页表基地址寄存器）
	TTBR0 / TTBR1
	存的是：
	页表在 DDR 里的“起始地址”
2️⃣ TLB（快表）
Translation Lookaside Buffer
缓存最近用过的地址映射（加速用）


当 CPU 执行：
*(volatile u32 *)0xFED10000 = val;
1️⃣ CPU发出虚拟地址 VA（0xFED10000）
2️⃣ 先查 TLB
    ✔ 命中 → 直接得到物理地址
    ✖ 未命中 → 走页表
3️⃣ 访问 DDR 中的页表（通过 TTBR）
4️⃣ 解析页表项（PTE）
5️⃣ 得到物理地址 PA（0x20010000）
6️⃣ 访问外设寄存器

ioremap 干的事情
void __iomem *ioremap(phys, size);
内部做：
1️⃣ 找一段空闲虚拟地址
vmalloc 区域
2️⃣ 修改页表
VA → PA
3️⃣ 设置属性
MT_DEVICE（不缓存）
4️⃣ 刷新 TLB
让 CPU 立刻生效

./arch/arm/include/asm/io.h:159:#define IOMEM(x)        ((void __force __iomem *)(x)) //c语言用
./arch/arm/include/asm/assembler.h:27:#define IOMEM(x)  (x)  //汇编用


include\linux\rockchip\iomap.h
#define RK_IO_ADDRESS(x)                IOMEM(0xFED00000 + x)
#define RK_GRF_VIRT                     RK_IO_ADDRESS(0x00010000)



arch\arm\mach-rockchip\rk312x.c
#define RK312X_DEVICE(name) \
	{ \
		.virtual	= (unsigned long) RK_##name##_VIRT, \
		.pfn		= __phys_to_pfn(RK312X_##name##_PHYS), \
		.length		= RK312X_##name##_SIZE, \
		.type		= MT_DEVICE, \
	}


static struct map_desc rk312x_io_desc[] __initdata = {
	RK312X_DEVICE(CRU),
	RK312X_DEVICE(GRF),
	RK312X_DEVICE(ROM),
	RK312X_DEVICE(PMU),
	RK312X_DEVICE(EFUSE),

	RK312X_DEVICE(CPU_AXI_BUS),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_DEBUG_UART_VIRT, RK312X_UART2_PHYS, RK312X_UART_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_DDR_VIRT, RK312X_DDR_PCTL_PHYS, RK312X_DDR_PCTL_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_DDR_VIRT + RK312X_DDR_PCTL_SIZE, RK312X_DDR_PHY_PHYS, RK312X_DDR_PHY_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GPIO_VIRT(0), RK312X_GPIO0_PHYS, RK312X_GPIO_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GPIO_VIRT(1), RK312X_GPIO1_PHYS, RK312X_GPIO_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GPIO_VIRT(2), RK312X_GPIO2_PHYS, RK312X_GPIO_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GPIO_VIRT(3), RK312X_GPIO3_PHYS, RK312X_GPIO_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GIC_VIRT, RK312X_GIC_DIST_PHYS, RK312X_GIC_DIST_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_GIC_VIRT + RK312X_GIC_DIST_SIZE, RK312X_GIC_CPU_PHYS, RK312X_GIC_CPU_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK312X_IMEM_VIRT, RK312X_IMEM_PHYS, RK312X_IMEM_SIZE),
	RK_DEVICE(RK_PWM_VIRT, RK312X_PWM_PHYS, RK312X_PWM_SIZE),
};

include\linux\rockchip\iomap.h
#define RK3036_GRF_PHYS			0x20008000
#define RK312X_GRF_PHYS                 RK3036_GRF_PHYS

内核驱动注册属性接口
1.定义属性的宏
static CLASS_ATTR(otg_hw_ctl, 0664, show_fn, store_fn); 
宏展开
struct class_attribute class_attr_otg_hw_ctl = {
    .attr = { .name = "otg_hw_ctl", .mode = 0664 },
    .show = show_fn,
    .store = store_fn,
};
	
otg_drv_class = class_create(THIS_MODULE, "otg_hw_ctl");
class_create_file(otg_drv_class, &class_attr_otg_hw_ctl);
/sys/class/... 下创建文件
        ↓
用户空间可读写





1.
module_param_named(name, variable, type, perm);
“定义一个 模块参数 name，它映射到变量 variable”
| 参数       | 作用                       |
| -------- | ------------------------ |
| name     | 用户看到/设置的参数名              |
| variable | 内核里真正的变量                 |
| type     | 类型（int / bool / charp 等） |
| perm     | sysfs 权限（0444=只读）        |

2.
MODULE_PARM_DESC(name, "desc");
给参数加说明（会出现在 sysfs / modinfo）


1️⃣ 支持模块加载时传参
如果驱动是 .ko：
insmod dwc_otg.ko dma_enable=1 speed=0
这些参数会：
👉 写入 dwc_otg_module_params.xxx
2️⃣ 映射到 sysfs
加载后你会看到：
/sys/module/dwc_otg/parameters/
里面一堆：
dma_enable
speed
otg_cap
...
可以：
cat dma_enable
echo 1 > dma_enable   # 如果权限允许
3️⃣ 驱动内部直接用变量
比如：
if (dwc_otg_module_params.dma_enable) {
    // 走DMA模式
}




👉 driver_create_file() 的作用是：
在 sysfs 里给“驱动（driver）对象”创建一个属性文件
int driver_create_file(struct device_driver *drv,
                       const struct driver_attribute *attr);
例子：
driver_create_file(&dwc_otg_driver.driver, &driver_attr_version);
等价于：
👉 在 sysfs 里创建：
/sys/bus/platform/drivers/dwc_otg/version
Linux 设备模型层级：
bus（总线）
 └── driver（驱动）
      └── device（设备）
对应 sysfs：
/sys/bus/platform/
 └── drivers/
      └── dwc_otg/
           ├── version
           ├── debuglevel
           ├── ...
👉 driver_create_file() 就是往这里加文件
举个完整例子
比如：
static ssize_t version_show(struct device_driver *drv, char *buf)
{
    return sprintf(buf, "1.0\n");
}
static DRIVER_ATTR(version, 0444, version_show, NULL);
然后：
driver_create_file(&dwc_otg_driver.driver, &driver_attr_version);

用户态看到的效果
cat /sys/bus/platform/drivers/dwc_otg/version
输出：
1.0


七、一个更直观的理解

你可以把 .data 理解为：



一、
.data = &usb20otg_pdata_rk3126
👉 本质是：
“匹配成功后，顺便带一份 SoC 私有配置数据”
二、这个 data 是怎么用的
在 probe 里通常会这样写：
const struct of_device_id *match;
match = of_match_device(usb20_otg_of_match, &pdev->dev);
if (match) {
    pdata = match->data;
}
三、整个流程
设备树：
    compatible = "rockchip,rk3126_usb20_otg"
        ↓ 匹配
usb20_otg_of_match[]：
    找到 rk3126 项
        ↓
.data = &usb20otg_pdata_rk3126
        ↓
probe():
    拿到 pdata
        ↓
驱动根据 pdata 初始化硬件





res_base = platform_get_resource(_dev, IORESOURCE_MEM, 0);
“从设备描述里，拿第 0 个内存资源（寄存器地址范围）”
struct resource {
    resource_size_t start;  // 起始物理地址
    resource_size_t end;    // 结束地址
    unsigned long flags;    // 类型（MEM / IRQ 等）
};

从设备树中获取
usb_otg: usb@10180000 {
    compatible = "rockchip,rk3126_usb20_otg";
    reg = <0x10180000 0x10000>;
};

index = 0 第 0 个内存资源
reg = <0x10180000 0x10000>,
      <0x10190000 0x1000>;
| index | 地址         |
| ----- | ---------- |
| 0     | 0x10180000 |
| 1     | 0x10190000 |

下一步一定是：
1️⃣ request_mem_region（可选）
request_mem_region(res->start, size, "dwc_otg");
👉 声明“这块内存我用了”
2️⃣ ioremap（关键）
void __iomem *base;
base = ioremap(res->start, resource_size(res));
👉 把 物理地址 → 虚拟地址
3️⃣ 访问寄存器
readl(base + offset);
writel(val, base + offset);



驱动中使用中断：
硬件路径：
EHCI 控制器
    ↓
IRQ 引脚
    ↓
GIC / 中断控制器
    ↓
CPU
    ↓
Linux IRQ 子系统
    ↓
ehci_irq()
从设备树上获取中断号
irq = platform_get_irq(pdev, 0);
把 ehci_irq 绑定到这个 IRQ 号
request_irq(irq, ehci_irq, ...);
✔ 2：打开中断开关（关键！）
writel(USBSTS_INT | USBSTS_ERR | USBSTS_PCD,
       &ehci->regs->intr_enable);


usb host ehci 流程图
[插入设备]
    ↓
PORTSC.CCS = 1
    ↓
USBSTS.PORT_CHANGE = 1
    ↓
IRQ触发
    ↓
ehci_irq()
    ↓
hub_port_connect_change()
    ↓
PORT_RESET
    ↓
PORTSC.PE = 1
    ↓
Set Address
    ↓
Get Descriptor
    ↓
加载驱动(Linux 根据：VID / PID / class 匹配驱动：U盘、键盘、串口)
    ↓
设备可用



usb_control {
	compatible = "rockchip,rk3126-usb-control";
	host_drv_gpio = <0xa5 0x14 0x1>;
	otg_drv_gpio = <0xa5 0x11 0x1>;
	rockchip,remote_wakeup;
	rockchip,usb_irq_wakeup;
};

host_drv_gpio：
<0xa5 0x14 0x1>
→ gpio3 GPIO_C4 GPIO_ACTIVE_LOW

otg_drv_gpio:
<0xa5 0x11 0x1>
→ gpio3 GPIO_C1 GPIO_ACTIVE_LOW

 SCSI = Small Computer System Interface

 U盘（USB）
   ↓
usb-storage 驱动
   ↓
👉 转换成 SCSI 协议
   ↓
SCSI 子系统
   ↓
sd 驱动
   ↓
/dev/sda


👉 sd = SCSI Disk
sd 驱动 = SCSI 磁盘驱动
把 SCSI 设备变成：
/dev/sda
/dev/sdb
/dev/sdc


老式SCSI硬盘 = SCSI协议 + SCSI物理接口（并行总线）
Linux里的SCSI = 只保留“协议层”

[   52.637852] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: result = 0x1105 = -43776
[   52.644197] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: port 1 reset error -110
[   52.650671] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: wIndex = 0x1 , ports = 1


PORTSC

0x1105 = 0001 0001 0000 0101
| 位     | 名字   | 含义          |
| ----- | ---- | ----------- |
| bit0  | CCS  | 当前设备连接      |
| bit1  | CSC  | 连接状态变化      |
| bit2  | PE   | Port Enable |
| bit3  | PEC  | Enable变化    |
| bit4  | OCA  | 过流          |
| bit5  | OCC  | 过流变化        |
| bit6  | FPR  | resume      |
| bit7  | SUSP | suspend     |
| bit8  | PR   | reset       |
| bit12 | PP   | Port Power  |
| bit13 | PO   | Port Owner  |



二、USB Reset 时 D+ / D- 应该长什么样？
标准 USB2.0 reset 行为：

👉 Host 会把 D+ 和 D- 都拉低（SE0 状态）


✅ 3. reset 结束后状态

根据设备不同：

🔹 Full Speed 设备
D+ 被上拉（≈3.3V）
D- 低
🔹 Low Speed 设备
D- 被上拉
D+ 低


Reset结束后：




[   52.637852] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: result = 0x1105 = -43776
[    6.443006] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: result = 0x1101 = -43776
[    6.443022] rockchip_ehci_host 101c0000.usb: result = 0x1005 = -43776

寄存器：
GRF_UOC1_CON5
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x0194) 


/* PORTSC: offset 0x44 */
port_status[0]
在 EHCI 规范里，这个寄存器叫：
PORTSC (Port Status and Control Register)
port_status[0] → 第 1 个 Root Hub 端口（Port 1）
port_status[1] → 第 2 个端口（如果有的话）

EHCI 寄存器是一个 内存映射寄存器块（MMIO），结构大概这样：
EHCI Base Address
│
├── Capability Registers (HC Cap)
│
└── Operational Registers (HC Op)   ← ehci->regs 指向这里
     │
     ├── USBCMD
     ├── USBSTS
     ├── USBINTR
     ├── FRINDEX
     ├── CTRLDSSEGMENT
     ├── PERIODICLISTBASE
     ├── ASYNCLISTADDR
     ├── CONFIGFLAG
     └── PORTSC[0]   ← 这个
     └── PORTSC[1]

👉 PORTSC[0] 的地址 =
EHCI Operational Base + 0x44
👉 PORTSC[n]：
EHCI Operational Base + 0x44 + (n * 4)

三、代码里的 ehci->regs，在 Linux EHCI 驱动里：
struct ehci_regs {
    u32 command;        // 0x00
    u32 status;         // 0x04
    u32 intr_enable;    // 0x08
    u32 frame_index;    // 0x0c
    u32 segment;        // 0x10
    u32 frame_list;     // 0x14
    u32 async_next;     // 0x18
    u32 reserved[9];    // 到 0x40
    u32 config_flag;    // 0x40
    u32 port_status[];  // 0x44 开始
};

usb_phy_init();
usb_phy_power_on();

ID pin 状态
dr_mode = "host"（如果是 dwc_otg）



       ┌──────────────┐
       │   EHCI 控制器 │
       └──────┬───────┘
              │
              │  UTMI接口（数字信号）
              │
       ┌──────▼───────┐
       │    USB PHY    │  
       └──────┬───────┘
              │
              │ 模拟信号
              │
            D+ / D-

SE0 = Single-Ended Zero
状态	DP	DM	含义
J-state	1	0	空闲（Full-Speed）
K-state	0	1	Resume / Low-Speed idle
SE0	0	0	❗无设备 / Reset
SE1	1	1	非法状态

根本原因
您的EHCI控制器在初始化后，端口被设置为挂起状态（PORT_SUSPEND = 1），而且重新授权根集线器并不会自动唤醒挂起的端口。挂起状态下的端口不会响应设备插入事件，因此热插拔无效。

建议优先尝试方案2（直接写寄存器唤醒），这是最快验证硬件是否正常的方法。如果写寄存器能唤醒端口，那么就可以在驱动中永久修复这个问题。



# 1. 完全断开并重新连接根集线器
echo -n "0" > /sys/bus/usb/devices/usb1/authorized
sleep 1
echo -n "1" > /sys/bus/usb/devices/usb1/authorized
sleep 1

# 2. 强制重新扫描
echo -n "1" > /sys/bus/usb/devices/usb1/authorized_default

# 3. 手动触发hub事件（如果支持）
echo -n "1" > /sys/bus/usb/devices/usb1/1-0:1.0/authorized 2>/dev/null

# 4. 检查端口状态
cat /sys/kernel/debug/usb/ehci/101c0000.usb/registers 2>/dev/null

# 5. 最后尝试插入U盘并观察是否有中断
# 同时在内核中查看是否有新消息
dmesg | tail -f



1查一下为啥没有唤醒端口

2看一下，端口什么时候被挂起的

3.看下现有的程序端口什么条件被唤醒

用户空间可以控制root hub重启

struct ehci_hcd {			/* one per controller */
	/* timing support */
	enum ehci_hrtimer_event	next_hrtimer_event;
	unsigned		enabled_hrtimer_events;
	ktime_t			hr_timeouts[EHCI_HRTIMER_NUM_EVENTS];
	struct hrtimer		hrtimer;

	int			PSS_poll_count;
	int			ASS_poll_count;
	int			died_poll_count;

	/* glue to PCI and HCD framework */
	struct ehci_caps __iomem *caps;
	struct ehci_regs __iomem *regs;
	struct ehci_dbg_port __iomem *debug;

	__u32			hcs_params;	/* cached register copy */
	spinlock_t		lock;
	enum ehci_rh_state	rh_state;

	/* general schedule support */
	bool			scanning:1;
	bool			need_rescan:1;
	bool			intr_unlinking:1;
	bool			iaa_in_progress:1;
	bool			async_unlinking:1;
	bool			shutdown:1;
	struct ehci_qh		*qh_scan_next;

	/* async schedule support */
	struct ehci_qh		*async;
	struct ehci_qh		*dummy;		/* For AMD quirk use */
	struct list_head	async_unlink;
	struct list_head	async_idle;
	unsigned		async_unlink_cycle;
	unsigned		async_count;	/* async activity count */

	/* periodic schedule support */
#define	DEFAULT_I_TDPS		1024		/* some HCs can do less */
	unsigned		periodic_size;
	__hc32			*periodic;	/* hw periodic table */
	dma_addr_t		periodic_dma;
	struct list_head	intr_qh_list;
	unsigned		i_thresh;	/* uframes HC might cache */

	union ehci_shadow	*pshadow;	/* mirror hw periodic table */
	struct list_head	intr_unlink;
	unsigned		intr_unlink_cycle;
	unsigned		now_frame;	/* frame from HC hardware */
	unsigned		last_iso_frame;	/* last frame scanned for iso */
	unsigned		intr_count;	/* intr activity count */
	unsigned		isoc_count;	/* isoc activity count */
	unsigned		periodic_count;	/* periodic activity count */
	unsigned		uframe_periodic_max; /* max periodic time per uframe */


	/* list of itds & sitds completed while now_frame was still active */
	struct list_head	cached_itd_list;
	struct ehci_itd		*last_itd_to_free;
	struct list_head	cached_sitd_list;
	struct ehci_sitd	*last_sitd_to_free;

	/* per root hub port */
	unsigned long		reset_done [EHCI_MAX_ROOT_PORTS];

	/* bit vectors (one bit per port) */
	unsigned long		bus_suspended;		/* which ports were
			already suspended at the start of a bus suspend */
	unsigned long		companion_ports;	/* which ports are
			dedicated to the companion controller */
	unsigned long		owned_ports;		/* which ports are
			owned by the companion during a bus suspend */
	unsigned long		port_c_suspend;		/* which ports have
			the change-suspend feature turned on */
	unsigned long		suspended_ports;	/* which ports are
			suspended */
	unsigned long		resuming_ports;		/* which ports have
			started to resume */

	/* per-HC memory pools (could be per-bus, but ...) */
	struct dma_pool		*qh_pool;	/* qh per active urb */
	struct dma_pool		*qtd_pool;	/* one or more per qh */
	struct dma_pool		*itd_pool;	/* itd per iso urb */
	struct dma_pool		*sitd_pool;	/* sitd per split iso urb */

	unsigned		random_frame;
	unsigned long		next_statechange;
	ktime_t			last_periodic_enable;
	u32			command;

	/* SILICON QUIRKS */
	unsigned		no_selective_suspend:1;
	unsigned		has_fsl_port_bug:1; /* FreeScale */
	unsigned		big_endian_mmio:1;
	unsigned		big_endian_desc:1;
	unsigned		big_endian_capbase:1;
	unsigned		has_amcc_usb23:1;
	unsigned		need_io_watchdog:1;
	unsigned		amd_pll_fix:1;
	unsigned		use_dummy_qh:1;	/* AMD Frame List table quirk*/
	unsigned		has_synopsys_hc_bug:1; /* Synopsys HC */
	unsigned		frame_index_bug:1; /* MosChip (AKA NetMos) */
	unsigned		need_oc_pp_cycle:1; /* MPC834X port power */
	unsigned		imx28_write_fix:1; /* For Freescale i.MX28 */

	/* required for usb32 quirk */
	#define OHCI_CTRL_HCFS          (3 << 6)
	#define OHCI_USB_OPER           (2 << 6)
	#define OHCI_USB_SUSPEND        (3 << 6)

	#define OHCI_HCCTRL_OFFSET      0x4
	#define OHCI_HCCTRL_LEN         0x4
	__hc32			*ohci_hcctrl_reg;
	unsigned		has_hostpc:1;
	unsigned		has_ppcd:1; /* support per-port change bits */
	u8			sbrn;		/* packed release number */

	/* irq statistics */
#ifdef EHCI_STATS
	struct ehci_stats	stats;
#	define COUNT(x) do { (x)++; } while (0)
#else
#	define COUNT(x) do {} while (0)
#endif

	/* debug files */
#ifdef DEBUG
	struct dentry		*debug_dir;
#endif

	/* platform-specific data -- must come last */
	unsigned long		priv[0] __aligned(sizeof(s64));
};

static void __init rk312x_init_suspend(void)
{
	pr_info("%s\n", __func__);
	rkpm_pie_init();
	rk312x_suspend_init();
}


在这个区间：



[    7.722177] initcall clk_disable_unused+0x0/0x104


CMDLINE:console=ttyS2,115200 clk_ignore_unused earlyprintk mtdparts=rk29xxnand:0x00002000@0x00002000(uboot),0x00002000@0x00004000(misc),0x00008000@0x00006000(resource),0x00010000@0x0000E000(boot),0x00020000@0x0001E000(backup),-@0x0003E000(linuxroot)

clk_disable_unused()

	b.驱动代码中修改
	改成：
	static void usb20ehci_clock_init(void *pdata)
	{
		struct rkehci_platform_data *usbpdata = pdata;
		struct clk *ahbclk, *phyclk;
		struct clk *ahbclk1;

		ahbclk1 = devm_clk_get(usbpdata->dev, "hclk_host0_3126b");
		if (IS_ERR(ahbclk1)) {
			dev_err(usbpdata->dev, "Failed to get hclk_host0_3126b\n");
			return;
		}
		ahbclk = devm_clk_get(usbpdata->dev, "hclk_host0");
		if (IS_ERR(ahbclk)) {
			dev_err(usbpdata->dev, "Failed to get hclk_usb1\n");
			return;
		}

		phyclk = devm_clk_get(usbpdata->dev, "clk_usbphy0");
		if (IS_ERR(phyclk)) {
			dev_err(usbpdata->dev, "Failed to get clk_usbphy0\n");
			return;
		}

		usbpdata->phyclk = phyclk;
		usbpdata->ahbclk = ahbclk;
		usbpdata->ahbclk1 = ahbclk1;
		printk(KERN_INFO "xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxEHCI: %s ok\n", __func__);
	}

	
	static void usb20otg_clock_init(void *pdata)
	{
		struct dwc_otg_platform_data *usbpdata = pdata;
		struct clk *ahbclk, *phyclk;

		ahbclk = devm_clk_get(usbpdata->dev, "hclk_usb0");
		if (IS_ERR(ahbclk)) {
			dev_err(usbpdata->dev, "Failed to get hclk_usb0\n");
			return;
		}

		phyclk = devm_clk_get(usbpdata->dev, "clk_usbphy1");
		if (IS_ERR(phyclk)) {
			dev_err(usbpdata->dev, "Failed to get clk_usbphy1\n");
			return;
		}

		usbpdata->phyclk = phyclk;
		usbpdata->ahbclk = ahbclk;
	}

这里有个bug，需要改成下方这样：

		} else if (win->id == 2) {
			mask = m_HWC_EN | m_HWC_LODAD_EN;
			val = v_HWC_EN(win->state) | v_HWC_LODAD_EN(1);
			lcdc_msk_reg(lcdc_dev, SYS_CTRL, mask, val);
			if ((win->area[0].xsize == 32) &&
			    (win->area[0].ysize == 32))
				hwc_size = 0;
			else if ((win->area[0].xsize == 64) &&
				 (win->area[0].ysize == 64))
				hwc_size = 1;
			else
				dev_err(lcdc_dev->dev, "unsupport hwc size:x=%d,y=%d\n",
					win->area[0].xsize, win->area[0].ysize);
			lcdc_writel(lcdc_dev, HWC_DSP_ST,
				    v_DSP_STX(win->area[0].dsp_stx) |
				    v_DSP_STY(win->area[0].dsp_sty));
			// 增加下面这行
			lcdc_msk_reg(lcdc_dev, SYS_CTRL,
						m_HWC_SIZE,
						v_HWC_SIZE(hwc_size));
			// 到这里结束
			lcdc_writel(lcdc_dev, HWC_MST, win->area[0].y_addr);
		}
	}

//usb camera 支持的像素格式及分辨率
Pixel format: YUYV
Pixel format: MJPG
Pixel format: NV12
Resolution: 640x480
Resolution: 1920x1080
Resolution: 1280x960
Resolution: 1280x720

注册uvc驱动：
drivers\media\usb\uvc\uvc_driver.c

驱动ioctrl入口：
drivers\media\usb\uvc\uvc_v4l2.c
这个 uvc_v4l2.c 文件是 UVC 驱动中负责对接 Linux 内核 V4L2 框架的“适配层”或“接口层”。
它在 UVC 硬件逻辑和 V4L2 标准用户态接口之间起到了翻译官和协议转换器的作用。


UVC 驱动的底层视频流处理核心，位于 uvc_v4l2.c（适配层）的更下一层:
drivers\media\usb\uvc\uvc_video.c
它的核心职责是：通过 USB 总线搬运实际的视频数据。可以把它理解为 UVC 驱动中的“数据搬运工”和“硬件协议执行者”


drivers\usb\core\message.c
drivers\usb\core\urb.c
drivers\usb\core\hcd.c

drivers\media\usb\uvc\uvc_queue.c
drivers\media\v4l2-core\videobuf2-core.c


//ion 零拷贝
在这里添加头文件：
drivers\media\usb\uvc\uvc_queue.c
#include <media/videobuf2-dma-contig.h>  // 添加这行

//修改 drivers\media\usb\uvc\Kconfig
隐藏的 tristate（无 prompt）：不能由用户直接选择，只能被其他选项的 select 或依赖关系自动决定
config USB_VIDEO_CLASS
	tristate "USB Video Class (UVC)"
	select VIDEOBUF2_VMALLOC
	select VIDEOBUF2_DMA_CONTIG # 添加这一行
	---help---
	  Support for the USB Video Class (UVC).  Currently only video
	  input devices, such as webcams, are supported.

	  For more information see: <http://linux-uvc.berlios.de/>
//启用：
CONFIG_VIDEOBUF2_DMA_CONTIG=y
//修改这里：
int uvc_queue_init(struct uvc_video_queue *queue, enum v4l2_buf_type type,
		    int drop_corrupted)
{
	int ret;

	queue->queue.type = type;
	queue->queue.io_modes = VB2_MMAP | VB2_USERPTR | VB2_DMABUF;
	queue->queue.drv_priv = queue;
	queue->queue.buf_struct_size = sizeof(struct uvc_buffer);
	queue->queue.ops = &uvc_queue_qops;
	// queue->queue.mem_ops = &vb2_vmalloc_memops;
	queue->queue.mem_ops = &vb2_dma_contig_memops; // xxxxxx 修改
	queue->queue.alloc_ctx = &queue->dev;   // xxxxxxxxxxx 新增
	queue->queue.timestamp_type = V4L2_BUF_FLAG_TIMESTAMP_MONOTONIC;
	ret = vb2_queue_init(&queue->queue);
	if (ret)
		return ret;

	mutex_init(&queue->mutex);
	spin_lock_init(&queue->irqlock);
	INIT_LIST_HEAD(&queue->irqqueue);
	queue->flags = drop_corrupted ? UVC_QUEUE_DROP_CORRUPTED : 0;

	return 0;
}

这个函数里新增一行：

int uvc_video_init(struct uvc_streaming *stream)
{
	printk(KERN_INFO "xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxuvc_video_init: stream %p\n", stream);
	dump_stack();
	struct uvc_streaming_control *probe = &stream->ctrl;
	struct uvc_format *format = NULL;
	struct uvc_frame *frame = NULL;
	unsigned int i;
	int ret;

	if (stream->nformats == 0) {
		uvc_printk(KERN_INFO, "No supported video formats found.\n");
		return -EINVAL;
	}

	atomic_set(&stream->active, 0);
	printk(KERN_INFO "uvc_video_init: stream->type %d\n", stream->type);
	/* Initialize the video buffers queue. */
	stream->queue.dev = &stream->dev->udev->dev;   // xxxxxx新增
	ret = uvc_queue_init(&stream->queue, stream->type, !uvc_no_drop_param);
	if (ret)
		return ret;

	/* Alternate setting 0 should be the default, yet the XBox Live Vision
	 * Cam (and possibly other devices) crash or otherwise misbehave if
	 * they don't receive a SET_INTERFACE request before any other video
	 * control request.
	 */
	usb_set_interface(stream->dev->udev, stream->intfnum, 0);

	/* Set the streaming probe control with default streaming parameters
	 * retrieved from the device. Webcams that don't suport GET_DEF
	 * requests on the probe control will just keep their current streaming
	 * parameters.
	 */
	if (uvc_get_video_ctrl(stream, probe, 1, UVC_GET_DEF) == 0)
		uvc_set_video_ctrl(stream, probe, 1);

	/* Initialize the streaming parameters with the probe control current
	 * value. This makes sure SET_CUR requests on the streaming commit
	 * control will always use values retrieved from a successful GET_CUR
	 * request on the probe control, as required by the UVC specification.
	 */
	ret = uvc_get_video_ctrl(stream, probe, 1, UVC_GET_CUR);
	if (ret < 0)
		return ret;

	/* Check if the default format descriptor exists. Use the first
	 * available format otherwise.
	 */
	for (i = stream->nformats; i > 0; --i) {
		format = &stream->format[i-1];
		if (format->index == probe->bFormatIndex)
			break;
	}

	if (format->nframes == 0) {
		uvc_printk(KERN_INFO, "No frame descriptor found for the "
			"default format.\n");
		return -EINVAL;
	}

	/* Zero bFrameIndex might be correct. Stream-based formats (including
	 * MPEG-2 TS and DV) do not support frames but have a dummy frame
	 * descriptor with bFrameIndex set to zero. If the default frame
	 * descriptor is not found, use the first available frame.
	 */
	for (i = format->nframes; i > 0; --i) {
		frame = &format->frame[i-1];
		if (frame->bFrameIndex == probe->bFrameIndex)
			break;
	}

	probe->bFormatIndex = format->index;
	probe->bFrameIndex = frame->bFrameIndex;

	stream->def_format = format;
	stream->cur_format = format;
	stream->cur_frame = frame;

	/* Select the video decoding function */
	if (stream->type == V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE) {
		if (stream->dev->quirks & UVC_QUIRK_BUILTIN_ISIGHT)
			stream->decode = uvc_video_decode_isight;
		else if (stream->intf->num_altsetting > 1)
			stream->decode = uvc_video_decode_isoc;
		else
			stream->decode = uvc_video_decode_bulk;
	} else {
		if (stream->intf->num_altsetting == 1)
			stream->decode = uvc_video_encode_bulk;
		else {
			uvc_printk(KERN_INFO, "Isochronous endpoints are not "
				"supported for video output devices.\n");
			return -EINVAL;
		}
	}

	return 0;
}

struct uvc_video_queue {
	struct vb2_queue queue;
	struct mutex mutex;	/* Protects queue */

	unsigned int flags;
	__u32 sequence;

	unsigned int buf_used;

	spinlock_t irqlock;	/* Protects flags and irqqueue */
	struct list_head irqqueue;
	struct device *dev;   // xxxxxxxxxxx 新增
};

struct v4l2_buffer {
	__u32			index;
	__u32			type;
	__u32			bytesused;
	__u32			flags;
	__u32			field;
	struct timeval		timestamp;
	struct v4l2_timecode	timecode;
	__u32			sequence;

	/* memory location */
	__u32			memory;
	union {
		__u32           offset;
		unsigned long   userptr;
		struct v4l2_plane *planes;
		__s32		fd;
	} m;
	__u32			length;
	__u32			reserved2;
	__u32			reserved;
};

struct vb2_plane {
	void			*mem_priv;
	struct dma_buf		*dbuf;
	unsigned int		dbuf_mapped;
};

struct vb2_buffer {
	struct v4l2_buffer	v4l2_buf;
	struct v4l2_plane	v4l2_planes[VIDEO_MAX_PLANES];

	struct vb2_queue	*vb2_queue;

	unsigned int		num_planes;

/* Private: internal use only */
	enum vb2_buffer_state	state;

	struct list_head	queued_entry;
	struct list_head	done_entry;

	struct vb2_plane	planes[VIDEO_MAX_PLANES];
};

struct vb2_ops {
	int (*queue_setup)(struct vb2_queue *q, const struct v4l2_format *fmt,
			   unsigned int *num_buffers, unsigned int *num_planes,
			   unsigned int sizes[], void *alloc_ctxs[]);

	void (*wait_prepare)(struct vb2_queue *q);
	void (*wait_finish)(struct vb2_queue *q);

	int (*buf_init)(struct vb2_buffer *vb);
	int (*buf_prepare)(struct vb2_buffer *vb);
	int (*buf_finish)(struct vb2_buffer *vb);
	void (*buf_cleanup)(struct vb2_buffer *vb);

	int (*start_streaming)(struct vb2_queue *q, unsigned int count);
	int (*stop_streaming)(struct vb2_queue *q);

	void (*buf_queue)(struct vb2_buffer *vb);
};

struct vb2_queue {
	enum v4l2_buf_type		type;
	unsigned int			io_modes;
	unsigned int			io_flags;
	struct mutex			*lock;
	struct v4l2_fh			*owner;

	const struct vb2_ops		*ops;
	const struct vb2_mem_ops	*mem_ops;
	void				*drv_priv;
	unsigned int			buf_struct_size;
	u32				timestamp_type;
	gfp_t				gfp_flags;

/* private: internal use only */
	enum v4l2_memory		memory;
	struct vb2_buffer		*bufs[VIDEO_MAX_FRAME];
	unsigned int			num_buffers;

	struct list_head		queued_list;

	atomic_t			queued_count;
	struct list_head		done_list;
	spinlock_t			done_lock;
	wait_queue_head_t		done_wq;

	void				*alloc_ctx[VIDEO_MAX_PLANES];
	unsigned int			plane_sizes[VIDEO_MAX_PLANES];

	unsigned int			streaming:1;

	struct vb2_fileio_data		*fileio;
};

struct uvc_streaming {
	struct list_head list;
	struct uvc_device *dev;
	struct video_device *vdev;
	struct uvc_video_chain *chain;
	atomic_t active;

	struct usb_interface *intf;
	int intfnum;
	__u16 maxpsize;

	struct uvc_streaming_header header;
	enum v4l2_buf_type type;

	unsigned int nformats;
	struct uvc_format *format;

	struct uvc_streaming_control ctrl;
	struct uvc_format *def_format;
	struct uvc_format *cur_format;
	struct uvc_frame *cur_frame;
	/* Protect access to ctrl, cur_format, cur_frame and hardware video
	 * probe control.
	 */
	struct mutex mutex;

	/* Buffers queue. */
	unsigned int frozen : 1;
	struct uvc_video_queue queue;
	void (*decode) (struct urb *urb, struct uvc_streaming *video,
			struct uvc_buffer *buf);

	/* Context data used by the bulk completion handler. */
	struct {
		__u8 header[256];
		unsigned int header_size;
		int skip_payload;
		__u32 payload_size;
		__u32 max_payload_size;
	} bulk;

	struct urb *urb[UVC_URBS];
	char *urb_buffer[UVC_URBS];
	dma_addr_t urb_dma[UVC_URBS];
	unsigned int urb_size;

	__u32 sequence;
	__u8 last_fid;

	struct tasklet_struct *tasklet[UVC_URBS];     /* ddl@rock-chips.com */
	atomic_t urb_state[UVC_URBS];

	/* debugfs */
	struct dentry *debugfs_dir;
	struct {
		struct uvc_stats_frame frame;
		struct uvc_stats_stream stream;
	} stats;

	/* Timestamps support. */
	struct uvc_clock {
		struct uvc_clock_sample {
			u32 dev_stc;
			u16 dev_sof;
			struct timespec host_ts;
			u16 host_sof;
		} *samples;

		unsigned int head;
		unsigned int count;
		unsigned int size;

		u16 last_sof;
		u16 sof_offset;

		spinlock_t lock;
	} clock;
};

struct video_device
{
#if defined(CONFIG_MEDIA_CONTROLLER)
	struct media_entity entity;
#endif
	/* device ops */
	const struct v4l2_file_operations *fops;

	/* sysfs */
	struct device dev;		/* v4l device */
	struct cdev *cdev;		/* character device */

	/* Set either parent or v4l2_dev if your driver uses v4l2_device */
	struct device *parent;		/* device parent */
	struct v4l2_device *v4l2_dev;	/* v4l2_device parent */

	/* Control handler associated with this device node. May be NULL. */
	struct v4l2_ctrl_handler *ctrl_handler;

	/* vb2_queue associated with this device node. May be NULL. */
	struct vb2_queue *queue;

	/* Priority state. If NULL, then v4l2_dev->prio will be used. */
	struct v4l2_prio_state *prio;

	/* device info */
	char name[32];
	int vfl_type;	/* device type */
	int vfl_dir;	/* receiver, transmitter or m2m */
	/* 'minor' is set to -1 if the registration failed */
	int minor;
	u16 num;
	/* use bitops to set/clear/test flags */
	unsigned long flags;
	/* attribute to differentiate multiple indices on one physical device */
	int index;

	/* V4L2 file handles */
	spinlock_t		fh_lock; /* Lock for all v4l2_fhs */
	struct list_head	fh_list; /* List of struct v4l2_fh */

	int debug;			/* Activates debug level*/

	/* Video standard vars */
	v4l2_std_id tvnorms;		/* Supported tv norms */
	v4l2_std_id current_norm;	/* Current tvnorm */

	/* callbacks */
	void (*release)(struct video_device *vdev);

	/* ioctl callbacks */
	const struct v4l2_ioctl_ops *ioctl_ops;
	DECLARE_BITMAP(valid_ioctls, BASE_VIDIOC_PRIVATE);

	/* serialization lock */
	DECLARE_BITMAP(disable_locking, BASE_VIDIOC_PRIVATE);
	struct mutex *lock;
};

/**
 * struct dma_buf - shared buffer object
 * @size: size of the buffer
 * @file: file pointer used for sharing buffers across, and for refcounting.
 * @attachments: list of dma_buf_attachment that denotes all devices attached.
 * @ops: dma_buf_ops associated with this buffer object.
 * @exp_name: name of the exporter; useful for debugging.
 * @list_node: node for dma_buf accounting and debugging.
 * @priv: exporter specific private data for this buffer object.
 */
struct dma_buf {
	size_t size;
	struct file *file;
	struct list_head attachments;
	const struct dma_buf_ops *ops;
	/* mutex to serialize list manipulation, attach/detach and vmap/unmap */
	struct mutex lock;
	unsigned vmapping_counter;
	void *vmap_ptr;
	const char *exp_name;
	struct list_head list_node;
	void *priv;
};

struct dma_buf *dma_buf_get(int fd)
{
	struct file *file;

	file = fget(fd);

	if (!file)
		return ERR_PTR(-EBADF);

	if (!is_dma_buf_file(file)) {
		fput(file);
		return ERR_PTR(-EINVAL);
	}

	return file->private_data;
}
EXPORT_SYMBOL_GPL(dma_buf_get);


struct ion_fd_data {
	ion_user_handle_t handle;
	int fd;
};


struct sg_table {
	struct scatterlist *sgl;	/* the list */
	unsigned int nents;		/* number of mapped entries */
	unsigned int orig_nents;	/* original size of list */
};


struct scatterlist {
#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG_SG
	unsigned long	sg_magic;
#endif
	unsigned long	page_link;
	unsigned int	offset;
	unsigned int	length;
	dma_addr_t	dma_address;
#ifdef CONFIG_NEED_SG_DMA_LENGTH
	unsigned int	dma_length;
#endif
};


static inline struct page *sg_page(struct scatterlist *sg)
{
#ifdef CONFIG_DEBUG_SG
	BUG_ON(sg->sg_magic != SG_MAGIC);
	BUG_ON(sg_is_chain(sg));
#endif
	return (struct page *)((sg)->page_link & ~0x3);
}

static void *ion_dma_buf_vunmap(struct dma_buf *dmabuf)
{
	// printk(KERN_INFO, "ion_dma_buf_vmap: %p\n", dmabuf->priv);
	pr_info("xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx%s:  %p\n", __func__, dmabuf->priv);
	struct ion_buffer *buffer = dmabuf->priv;

	mutex_lock(&buffer->lock);
	ion_buffer_kmap_put(buffer);
	mutex_unlock(&buffer->lock);
}


struct ion_buffer {
	struct kref ref;
	union {
		struct rb_node node;
		struct list_head list;
	};
	struct ion_device *dev;
	struct ion_heap *heap;
	unsigned long flags;
	unsigned long private_flags;
	size_t size;
	union {
		void *priv_virt;
		ion_phys_addr_t priv_phys;
	};
	struct mutex lock;
	int kmap_cnt;
	void *vaddr;
	int dmap_cnt;
	struct sg_table *sg_table;
	struct page **pages;
	struct list_head vmas;
	/* used to track orphaned buffers */
	int handle_count;
	char task_comm[TASK_COMM_LEN];
	pid_t pid;
	unsigned int iommu_map_cnt;
	struct rb_root iommu_maps;
};

struct ion_heap {
	struct plist_node node;
	struct ion_device *dev;
	enum ion_heap_type type;
	struct ion_heap_ops *ops;
	unsigned long flags;
	unsigned int id;
	const char *name;
	struct shrinker shrinker;
	struct list_head free_list;
	size_t free_list_size;
	spinlock_t free_lock;
	wait_queue_head_t waitqueue;
	struct task_struct *task;
	int (*debug_show)(struct ion_heap *heap, struct seq_file *, void *);
};


struct ion_heap_ops {
	int (*allocate) (struct ion_heap *heap,
			 struct ion_buffer *buffer, unsigned long len,
			 unsigned long align, unsigned long flags);
	void (*free) (struct ion_buffer *buffer);
	int (*phys) (struct ion_heap *heap, struct ion_buffer *buffer,
		     ion_phys_addr_t *addr, size_t *len);
	struct sg_table *(*map_dma) (struct ion_heap *heap,
					struct ion_buffer *buffer);
	void (*unmap_dma) (struct ion_heap *heap, struct ion_buffer *buffer);
	void * (*map_kernel) (struct ion_heap *heap, struct ion_buffer *buffer);
	void (*unmap_kernel) (struct ion_heap *heap, struct ion_buffer *buffer);
	int (*map_user) (struct ion_heap *mapper, struct ion_buffer *buffer,
			 struct vm_area_struct *vma);
	int (*shrink)(struct ion_heap *heap, gfp_t gfp_mask, int nr_to_scan);
	int (*map_iommu)(struct ion_buffer *buffer,
				struct device *iommu_dev,
				struct ion_iommu_map *map_data,
				unsigned long iova_length,
				unsigned long flags);
	void (*unmap_iommu)(struct device *iommu_dev, struct ion_iommu_map *data);
};


enum {
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGBA_8888 = 1,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGBX_8888 = 2,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGB_888 = 3,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGB_565 = 4,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_BGRA_8888 = 5,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGBA_5551 = 6,
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_RGBA_4444 = 7,

	/* 0x8 - 0xFF range unavailable */

	/*
	 * 0x100 - 0x1FF
	 *
	 * This range is reserved for pixel formats that are specific to the HAL
	 * implementation.  Implementations can use any value in this range to
	 * communicate video pixel formats between their HAL modules.  These formats
	 * must not have an alpha channel.  Additionally, an EGLimage created from a
	 * gralloc buffer of one of these formats must be supported for use with the
	 * GL_OES_EGL_image_external OpenGL ES extension.
	 */

	/*
	 * Android YUV format:
	 *
	 * This format is exposed outside of the HAL to software decoders and
	 * applications.  EGLImageKHR must support it in conjunction with the
	 * OES_EGL_image_external extension.
	 *
	 * YV12 is a 4:2:0 YCrCb planar format comprised of a WxH Y plane followed
	 * by (W/2) x (H/2) Cr and Cb planes.
	 *
	 * This format assumes
	 * - an even width
	 * - an even height
	 * - a horizontal stride multiple of 16 pixels
	 * - a vertical stride equal to the height
	 *
	 *   y_size = stride * height
	 *   c_size = ALIGN(stride/2, 16) * height/2
	 *   size = y_size + c_size * 2
	 *   cr_offset = y_size
	 *   cb_offset = y_size + c_size
	 *
	 */
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YV12 = 0x32315659,	// YCrCb 4:2:0 Planar

	/* Legacy formats (deprecated), used by ImageFormat.java */
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCbCr_422_SP = 0x10,	// NV16
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_420_SP = 0x11,	// NV21
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCbCr_422_I = 0x14,	// YUY2
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_NV12 = 0x20,	// YUY2
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_NV12_VIDEO = 0x21,	// YUY2
	
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_NV12_10	    = 0x22, // YUV420_1obit
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCbCr_422_SP_10	= 0x23, // YUV422_1obit
	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_420_SP_10	= 0x24, //YUV444_1obit

	HAL_PIXEL_FORMAT_YCrCb_444 = 0x25,	//yuv444
	

};

enum data_format {
	ARGB888 = 0,
	RGB888,
	RGB565,
	YUV420 = 4,
	YUV422,
	YUV444,
	XRGB888,
	XBGR888,
	ABGR888,
	YUV420_A = 10,
	YUV422_A,
	YUV444_A,	
};

#define V4L2_MEMORY_DMABUF 4
#endif

#define FB_DEV      "/dev/fb0"
#define ION_DEV     "/dev/ion"
#define RGA_DEV     "/dev/rga"

#define VWIDTH 1280
#define VHEIGHT 720

// #define VWIDTH 640
// #define VHEIGHT 480

#define MYMEMTYPE V4L2_MEMORY_MMAP
// #define MYMEMTYPE V4L2_MEMORY_DMABUF

// #define BUFFSIZE (640 * 480 * 2)
#define BUFFSIZE (VWIDTH * VHEIGHT * 3 / 2)

struct fb_context {
    int fd;
    void *fbmem;
    size_t screensize;

    struct fb_var_screeninfo vinfo;
    struct fb_fix_screeninfo finfo;
};


struct ion_context {
    int ion_fd;
    int handle_fd;
    void *vaddr;
    unsigned long phys;
    size_t size;
};

struct ion_context ion_bg;
struct fb_context fb0;




int ion_alloc(struct ion_context *ctx, size_t size)
{
    ctx->size = size;

    struct ion_allocation_data alloc = {
        .len = size,
        .align = 0,
        .heap_id_mask = ION_HEAP_TYPE_DMA_MASK,
        .flags = 0,
    };

    if (ioctl(ctx->ion_fd, ION_IOC_ALLOC, &alloc) < 0) {
        perror("ION_IOC_ALLOC");
        return -1;
    }

    struct ion_fd_data fd_data = {0};
    fd_data.handle = alloc.handle;

    if (ioctl(ctx->ion_fd, ION_IOC_SHARE, &fd_data) < 0) {
        perror("ION_IOC_SHARE");
        return -1;
    }

    ctx->handle_fd = fd_data.fd;
    // printf("ion buffer allocated, handle fd: %d\n", ctx->handle_fd);
    fflush(stdout);


    return 0;
}

int map_ion_buffer(struct ion_context *ctx)
{
    ctx->vaddr = mmap(NULL,
                    ctx->size,
                    PROT_READ | PROT_WRITE,
                    MAP_SHARED,
                    ctx->handle_fd,
                    0);

    if (ctx->vaddr == MAP_FAILED) {
        perror("ion mmap");
        return -1;
    }
    // printf("ion buffer mapped %p\n", ctx->vaddr);
    return 0;
}
static inline long long time_us()
{
    struct timeval tv;
    gettimeofday(&tv, NULL);
    return (long long)tv.tv_sec * 1000000LL + tv.tv_usec;
}

static inline long long time_ms()
{
    return time_us() / 1000;
}
// struct ion_context ion_frames[4];



int init_fb(struct rk_fb_win_cfg_data *cfg)
{
    memset(cfg, 0, sizeof(*cfg));
    
    //bg
    cfg->wait_fs = 0;
    cfg->win_par[0].win_id = 0;
    cfg->win_par[0].z_order = 0;
    // cfg->win_par[0].mirror_en = 1;
    // cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].data_format = YUV420;    
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].data_format = FB_DATA_FMT;        
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].ion_fd = ion_bg.handle_fd;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].acq_fence_fd = -1;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].x_offset = 0; //缓冲区中的偏移，单位像素
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].y_offset = 0;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].xpos = 0; //屏幕上的位置，单位像素
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].ypos = 0;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].xsize = VWIDTH; //显示的宽高，单位像素
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].ysize = VHEIGHT;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].xact = VWIDTH; //缓冲区中的有效宽高，单位像素，不包含padding
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].yact = VHEIGHT;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].xvir = VWIDTH;  //缓冲区中实际的宽高，单位像素，包含可能因为对齐产生的padding
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].yvir = VHEIGHT;

    return 0;
}

int show_buffer(struct fb_context *fb, struct ion_context *ion, struct rk_fb_win_cfg_data *cfg)
{ 
    // cfg->win_par[1].area_par[0].ion_fd = ion->handle_fd;
    // cfg->win_par[1].area_par[0].acq_fence_fd = -1;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].ion_fd = ion->handle_fd;
    cfg->win_par[0].area_par[0].acq_fence_fd = -1;
    ioctl(fb->fd, RK_FBIOSET_CONFIG_DONE, cfg);
    int i;
    for ( i = 0; i < RK_MAX_BUF_NUM; i ++) {
        if (cfg->rel_fence_fd[i] >= 0) {
            // printf("cfg.rel_fence_fd[%d] = %d\n", i, cfg.rel_fence_fd[i]);
            close(cfg->rel_fence_fd[i]);
        }
    }
    if (cfg->ret_fence_fd >= 0) {
        // printf("cfg.ret_fence_fd = %d\n", cfg.ret_fence_fd);
        close(cfg->ret_fence_fd);
    }
    
    return 0;
}


int rga_blit(int fd_rga, int ion_fd_src, int ion_fd_dst, int s_x, int s_y, int d_x, int d_y, int act_w, int act_h, int vir_w_src, int vir_h_src, int vir_w_dst, int vir_h_dst, int alpha)
{
    struct rga_req req;
    memset(&req,0,sizeof(req));

    req.src.yrgb_addr = ion_fd_src;
    req.src.act_w = act_w;
    req.src.act_h = act_h;
    req.src.vir_w = vir_w_src;
    req.src.vir_h = vir_h_src;
    req.src.format = RK_FORMAT_YCbCr_420_SP;
    req.src.x_offset = s_x;
    req.src.y_offset = s_y;


    req.dst.yrgb_addr = ion_fd_dst;
    req.dst.act_w = act_w;
    req.dst.act_h = act_h;
    req.dst.format = RK_FORMAT_YCbCr_420_SP;
    req.dst.x_offset = d_x;
    req.dst.y_offset = d_y;
    req.dst.vir_w = vir_w_dst;
    req.dst.vir_h = vir_h_dst;

    // req.clip.xmin = 0;
    // req.clip.xmax = act_w - 1;
    // req.clip.ymin = 0;
    // req.clip.ymax = act_h - 1;

    req.clip.xmin = 0;
    req.clip.xmax = vir_w_dst - 1; 
    req.clip.ymin = 0;
    req.clip.ymax = vir_h_dst - 1;


    req.scale_mode = 1;
    // req.render_mode = bitblt_mode;
    req.rotate_mode = rotate_mode2;   // 水平镜像
    
    req.sina = 0;
    req.cosa = 0;
    // rga_req.rotate_mode = rotate_mode3; // 垂直镜像
    if (alpha) {
        req.alpha_rop_flag = 0
        | (1 << 0)  // bit0 = 1: alpha_rop_enable - 启用alpha混合
        | (0 << 1)  // bit1 = 0: rop enable - 禁用ROP光栅操作
        | (0 << 2)  // bit2 = 0: fading_enable - 禁用fading
        | (0 << 3)  // bit3 = 0: PD_enable - 禁用Porter-Duff（除非需要特殊混合模式）
        | (1 << 4)  // bit4 = 0: alpha cal_mode_sel - 选择alpha计算模式
        | (0 << 5)  // bit5 = 0: dither_enable - 禁用抖动
        | (0 << 6)  // bit6 = 0: gradient fill - 禁用渐变填充
        | (0 << 7); // bit7 = 0: AA_enable - 根据需要决定是否抗锯齿
        req.alpha_rop_mode = 0
        | (0x1 << 0)  // bit[0~1]: alpha模式 - 00表示使用源图像的alpha
        | (0x0 << 1)  // bit[0~1]: alpha模式 - 00表示使用源图像的alpha
        | (0x0 << 2)  // bit[2~3]: rop模式 - 不使用
        | (0x0 << 4)  // bit4: zero mode en - 禁用zero模式
        | (0x0 << 5); // bit5: dst alpha mode - 不使用目标alpha;

        req.alpha_global_value = 0xFF;  // 0x00~0xFF，0完全透明，0xFF完全不透明
    } else {
        req.alpha_rop_flag = 0;
    }
 
   
    // printf("=== RGA REQ ===\n");
    // printf("src: act=%dx%d vir=%dx%d offset=(%d,%d) fmt=%d addr=%d\n",
    //     req.src.act_w, req.src.act_h,
    //     req.src.vir_w, req.src.vir_h,
    //     req.src.x_offset, req.src.y_offset,
    //     req.src.format, req.src.yrgb_addr);
    // printf("dst: act=%dx%d vir=%dx%d offset=(%d,%d) fmt=%d addr=%d\n",
    //     req.dst.act_w, req.dst.act_h,
    //     req.dst.vir_w, req.dst.vir_h,
    //     req.dst.x_offset, req.dst.y_offset,
    //     req.dst.format, req.dst.yrgb_addr);
    // printf("clip: x=%d~%d y=%d~%d\n",
    //     req.clip.xmin, req.clip.xmax,
    //     req.clip.ymin, req.clip.ymax);
    // printf("rotate_mode=%d sina=%d cosa=%d\n",
        // req.rotate_mode, req.sina, req.cosa);
    // printf("sizeof(rga_req)=%zu\n", sizeof(struct rga_req));
    // fflush(stdout);

    ioctl(fd_rga, RGA_BLIT_SYNC, &req);

    return 0;
}


struct buffer {
    void   *start;   // mmap 后的虚拟地址
    size_t  length;  // buffer 大小
};
struct buffer *buffers;
unsigned int n_buffers;

int cnt = 1000;
struct ion_context ion_buf[2];
int idx = 0;
int main()
{
    int i;
    
    int fd_rga = open(RGA_DEV, O_RDWR);
    // 打开设备
    int cam_fd = open("/dev/video0", O_RDWR);
     // --------------- init ion --------------
    int ion_fd = open(ION_DEV, O_RDWR);
    if (ion_fd < 0) {
        perror("open ion");
        return -1;
    }
    ion_bg.ion_fd = ion_fd;
    ion_buf[0].ion_fd = ion_fd;
    ion_buf[1].ion_fd = ion_fd;
    // --------------- init fb ---------------
    fb0.fd = open(FB_DEV, O_RDWR);
    if (fb0.fd < 0) {
        perror("open fb0");
        return -1;
    }
    ioctl(fb0.fd, FBIOGET_FSCREENINFO, &fb0.finfo);
    ioctl(fb0.fd, FBIOGET_VSCREENINFO, &fb0.vinfo);
    fb0.screensize =
        fb0.vinfo.yres_virtual * fb0.finfo.line_length;


    // ----------------- alloc ion -----------------
    size_t size_bg = BUFFSIZE; 
    ion_alloc(&ion_bg, size_bg);    
    map_ion_buffer(&ion_bg);        
    ion_alloc(&ion_buf[0], size_bg);    
    map_ion_buffer(&ion_buf[0]);
    ion_alloc(&ion_buf[1], size_bg);    
    map_ion_buffer(&ion_buf[1]);
    // load_raw_to_ion(&ion_bg, "/usr/bin/desktop_bg_1280_720.raw", 0);
    // for (i = 0; i < 4; i++) {

    //     ion_frames[i].ion_fd = ion_fd;
    //     size_t size_bg = 640 * 480 * 2; // 640* 480, yuv422
    //     ion_alloc(&ion_frames[i], size_bg);
    //     map_ion_buffer(&ion_frames[i]);

    //     struct v4l2_buffer buf = {0};        
    //     buf.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
    //     buf.memory = MYMEMTYPE;
    //     buf.index = i;
    //     buf.m.fd = ion_frames[i].handle_fd;
    //     buf.length = size_bg;

    //     ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_QBUF, &buf);
    // }
    

    
    //
    struct rk_fb_win_cfg_data cfg;
    init_fb(&cfg);




        // while(cnt --) {
        //     idx ^= 1;
        //     int test_pix = rand() % 256;
        //     memset(ion_buf[idx].vaddr, test_pix, BUFFSIZE);

        //     cfg.win_par[0].area_par[0].ion_fd = ion_buf[idx].handle_fd;

        //     show_buffer(&fb0, &ion_buf[idx], &cfg);
        //     // for(i = 0; i < BUFFSIZE; i ++) {
        //     //     ((char*)(ion_bg.vaddr))[i] = test_pix;
        //     // }
        //     printf("xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxBuffer %d copied to ion buffer, showing on screen...\n", test_pix);
        //     // memset(ion_bg.vaddr, test_pix, BUFFSIZE);

        //     usleep(100000);
        // }





    // 查询支持的像素格式
    struct v4l2_fmtdesc fmtdesc;
    memset(&fmtdesc, 0, sizeof(fmtdesc));

    fmtdesc.index = 0;
    fmtdesc.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;

    while (ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_ENUM_FMT, &fmtdesc) == 0) {
        printf("Pixel format: %c%c%c%c\n", fmtdesc.pixelformat & 0xFF,
                                        (fmtdesc.pixelformat >> 8) & 0xFF,
                                        (fmtdesc.pixelformat >> 16) & 0xFF,
                                        (fmtdesc.pixelformat >> 24) & 0xFF);
        fmtdesc.index++;
    }

    // 查询支持的分辨率
    struct v4l2_frmsizeenum size;
    memset(&size, 0, sizeof(size));

    size.index = 0;
    size.pixel_format = V4L2PIXFMT;  // 选择对应的像素格式

    while (ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_ENUM_FRAMESIZES, &size) == 0) {
        printf("Resolution: %dx%d\n", size.discrete.width, size.discrete.height);
        size.index++;
    }

    // 设置像素格式
    struct v4l2_format fmt;
    memset(&fmt, 0, sizeof(fmt));

    fmt.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
    fmt.fmt.pix.width = VWIDTH;
    fmt.fmt.pix.height = VHEIGHT;
    // fmt.fmt.pix.pixelformat = V4L2_PIX_FMT_YUYV;  // 很关键
    fmt.fmt.pix.pixelformat = V4L2PIXFMT;  // 很关键
    fmt.fmt.pix.field = V4L2_FIELD_NONE;

    ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_S_FMT, &fmt);

    // 申请buffer
    struct v4l2_requestbuffers req = {0};
    req.count = 4;
    req.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
    req.memory = MYMEMTYPE;
    ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_REQBUFS, &req);

    buffers = calloc(req.count, sizeof(*buffers));
    n_buffers = req.count;

// mmp
for (i = 0; i < n_buffers; i++) {
    struct v4l2_buffer buf;
    memset(&buf, 0, sizeof(buf));

    buf.type   = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
    buf.memory = V4L2_MEMORY_MMAP;
    buf.index  = i;

    // 1️⃣ 向驱动查询 buffer 信息
    ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_QUERYBUF, &buf);

    // 2️⃣ 保存长度
    buffers[i].length = buf.length;

    // 3️⃣ mmap 映射到用户空间
    buffers[i].start = mmap(
        NULL,                   // 让系统自动分配地址
        buf.length,             // 映射大小
        PROT_READ | PROT_WRITE, // 可读写
        MAP_SHARED,             // 共享内存
        cam_fd,                     // 设备 fd
        buf.m.offset           // 偏移（关键！）
    );

    if (buffers[i].start == MAP_FAILED) {
        perror("mmap");
        exit(1);
    }
}




for (i = 0; i < 4; i++) {

        struct v4l2_buffer buf = {0};        
        buf.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
        buf.memory = MYMEMTYPE;
        buf.index = i;
        // buf.m.fd = ion_frames[i].handle_fd;
        buf.length = size_bg;

        ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_QBUF, &buf);
    }
    
   
    struct v4l2_queryctrl qc;

    qc.id = V4L2_CID_HFLIP;
    int ret = ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_QUERYCTRL, &qc);
if (ret == 0) {
    // printf("Camera supports horizontal flip control (V4L2_CID_HFLIP)\n");
    struct v4l2_control ctrl;

    ctrl.id = V4L2_CID_HFLIP;
    ctrl.value = 1;   // 1=镜像，0=正常

    ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_S_CTRL, &ctrl);
} else {
    // printf("Camera does NOT support horizontal flip control (V4L2_CID_HFLIP)\n");
}

    // 开始采集
    int type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
    ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_STREAMON, &type);


    while (1) {
        
        idx ^= 1;
        struct v4l2_buffer buf;
        memset(&buf, 0, sizeof(buf));

        buf.type = V4L2_BUF_TYPE_VIDEO_CAPTURE;
        buf.memory = MYMEMTYPE;

        // printf("loop in at %lld ms\n", time_ms());
        ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_DQBUF, &buf);

        // // printf("VIDIOC_DQBUF at %lld ms\n", time_ms());


        // int width = 640;
        // int height = 480;
        //printf("Captured frame: index=%d, bytesused=%d, length=%d, timecode=%d, type=%d, sequence=%d\n", buf.index, buf.bytesused, buf.length, buf.timecode, buf.type, buf.sequence);

        
        void *data = buffers[buf.index].start;
        int   len  = buf.bytesused;
        // printf("Frame data at %p, length %d\n", data, len);

        memcpy(ion_bg.vaddr, data, len);
        rga_blit(fd_rga, ion_bg.handle_fd, ion_buf[idx].handle_fd, 0, 0, 0, 0, VWIDTH, VHEIGHT, VWIDTH, VHEIGHT, VWIDTH, VHEIGHT, 0);


        
        
        // memset(ion_buf[idx].vaddr, test_pix, BUFFSIZE);

            // cfg.win_par[0].area_par[0].ion_fd = ion_buf[idx].handle_fd;

        show_buffer(&fb0, &ion_buf[idx], &cfg);






        // show_buffer(&fb0, &ion_frames[buf.index], &cfg);
        // show_buffer(&fb0, &ion_bg, &cfg);


        ioctl(cam_fd, VIDIOC_QBUF, &buf);
        
        // printf("VIDIOC_QBUF at %lld ms\n", time_ms());
    }


    return 0;
}

gmac: eth@2008c000 {
		compatible = "rockchip,rk312x-gmac";
		reg = <0x2008c000 0x4000>;

		compatible = "rockchip,rk_mmc", "rockchip,rk312x-sdmmc";
		reg = <0x10218000 0x4000>;
		interrupts = <GIC_SPI 15 IRQ_TYPE_LEVEL_HIGH>;
		#address-cells = <1>;
		#size-cells = <0>;
		pinctrl-names = "default","idle";
		pinctrl-0 = <&sdio0_pwren &sdio0_cmd &sdio0_clk &sdio0_bus4>;
		pinctrl-1 = <&sdio0_gpio>;
		clocks = <&clk_sdio>, <&clk_gates5 11>;
		clock-names = "clk_mmc", "hclk_mmc";
		dmas = <&pdma 11>;
		dma-names = "dw_mci";
		num-slots = <1>;
		fifo-depth = <0x100>;
		bus-width = <4>;
	        cru_regsbase = <0x124>;
		cru_reset_offset = <2>;
	};

mkdir -p ~/mali_test
cat > ~/mali_test/egl_test.c << 'EOF'
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <fcntl.h>
#include <unistd.h>

/* 只测试EGL初始化，不做实际渲染 */
#include <EGL/egl.h>

int main(void)
{
    EGLDisplay display;
    EGLint major, minor;

    printf("=== Mali EGL Test ===\n");

    /* 检查/dev/mali */
    int fd = open("/dev/mali", O_RDWR);
    if (fd < 0) {
        perror("open /dev/mali failed");
        return 1;
    }
    printf("[OK] /dev/mali opened, fd=%d\n", fd);
    close(fd);

    /* 检查/dev/ump */
    fd = open("/dev/ump", O_RDWR);
    if (fd < 0) {
        perror("open /dev/ump failed");
        return 1;
    }
    printf("[OK] /dev/ump opened, fd=%d\n", fd);
    close(fd);

    /* 初始化EGL */
    display = eglGetDisplay(EGL_DEFAULT_DISPLAY);
    if (display == EGL_NO_DISPLAY) {
        printf("[FAIL] eglGetDisplay failed\n");
        return 1;
    }
    printf("[OK] eglGetDisplay success\n");

    if (!eglInitialize(display, &major, &minor)) {
        printf("[FAIL] eglInitialize failed: 0x%x\n", eglGetError());
        return 1;
    }
    printf("[OK] eglInitialize success, EGL version %d.%d\n", major, minor);

    eglTerminate(display);
    printf("[OK] Done!\n");
    return 0;
}
EOF

arch\arm\kernel\sched_clock.c






################################################################################
#
# uboot-powkiddy-a13
#
################################################################################

UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_VERSION = powkiddy-a13
UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_SITE = \
    $(call github,alpgarcia,caesar-u-boot,$(UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_VERSION))
UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_LICENSE = GPLv2

UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_DEPENDENCIES = rk3128-blobs

define UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_BUILD_CMDS
    # FIXME: there should be a better way to build
    # Build uboot for wx8-rk3128
    cd $(@D) && ARCH=arm CHIP=rk3128 \
        CROSS_COMPILE=$(HOST_DIR)/bin/arm-buildroot-linux-gnueabihf- \
        make powkiddy-a13-rk3128_defconfig
    cd $(@D) && ARCH=arm CHIP=rk3128 \
        CROSS_COMPILE=$(HOST_DIR)/bin/arm-buildroot-linux-gnueabihf- make

    # Generate idbloader.img
    $(@D)/tools/mkimage -n rk3128 -T rksd -d \
        $(BINARIES_DIR)/rkbin/bin/rk31/rk3128_ddr_300MHz_v2.12.bin \
        $(@D)/idbloader.img
    cat $(BINARIES_DIR)/rkbin/bin/rk31/rk3128x_miniloader_v2.57.bin >> \
        $(@D)/idbloader.img

    # Generate uboot.img
    $(@D)/tools/loaderimage --pack --uboot $(@D)/u-boot-dtb.bin \
        $(@D)/uboot.img --size 1024 4
  
    # Generate trust.img
    $(@D)/tools/loaderimage --pack --trustos \
        $(BINARIES_DIR)/rkbin/bin/rk31/rk3126_tee_ta_v2.01.bin \
        $(@D)/trust.img --size 1024 4
endef

define UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13_INSTALL_TARGET_CMDS
	cp $(@D)/idbloader.img $(BINARIES_DIR)/idbloader.img
	cp $(@D)/uboot.img     $(BINARIES_DIR)/uboot-powkiddy-a13.img
	cp $(@D)/trust.img     $(BINARIES_DIR)/trust.img
endef

$(eval $(generic-package))

BR2_PACKAGE_HOST_MTOOLS=y

# spi flash support
BR2_PACKAGE_MTD=y

# Bootloader and Rotation
BR2_PACKAGE_UBOOT_PS5000=y
BR2_PACKAGE_UBOOT_PS7000=y
BR2_PACKAGE_UBOOT_POWKIDDY_A13=y
BR2_PACKAGE_RKBIN=y

# Misc
# BR2_PACKAGE_XOW is not set
BR2_PACKAGE_LIBCEC=y
BR2_PACKAGE_INPUT_EVENT_DAEMON=y
BR2_PACKAGE_LIBSODIUM=y
#BR2_PACKAGE_MOONLIGHT_EMBEDDED=n

export ARCH=arm
export CROSS_COMPILE=~/gcc-linaro-6.3.1-2017.05-i686_arm-linux-gnueabihf/bin/arm-linux-gnueabihf-

../rkbin/tools/loaderimage --pack --uboot ./u-boot.bin uboot.img 0x60000000
cp uboot.img /mnt/f/rk3128/

3.10版本pinctrl dts格式解析
struct iomux_mode{
        unsigned int mode:4,
                     off:4,
                     goff:4,
                     bank:4,
                     reserve:16;
};

struct union_mode{
        union{
                struct iomux_mode mux;
                unsigned int mode;
        };
};

kernel

总结一下这次调试发现的关键点：

libMali.so 软链接：Mali EGL 内部用 dlopen("libMali.so") 初始化，没有这个链接 EGL 完全不工作
EGL config id=5：RGB565 格式，是唯一真正可用的 window surface config
GBM 格式要用 GBM_FORMAT_RGB565：和 EGL config 匹配
drmModeAddFB 参数：RGB565 要用 depth=16, bpp=16
ES2 context 不可用：只能用 ES1 固定管线











---

### 必须的软链接

```bash
cd /usr/lib
ln -sf libmali.so libMali.so        # egl_linker_init 内部 dlopen 用大写M
ln -sf libmali.so libGLESv1_CM.so   # ES1
ln -sf libmali.so libGLESv2.so      # ES2，必须是 .so 不是 .so.2
ln -sf libmali.so libEGL.so
ln -sf libmali.so libgbm.so
```

### 关键参数

- GBM 格式用 `GBM_FORMAT_RGB565`
- EGL config id=5（RGB565 + WINDOW_BIT + ES1+ES2）
- drmModeAddFB 用 `depth=16, bpp=16`

### 问题根因

- `libMali.so` 缺失 → `eglGetDisplay` 返回 NULL
- `libGLESv2.so` 缺失（只有 `.so.2`）→ ES2 context 创建失败

fox /Fox.glb /Texture.png 2   # Run（跑步）

/* ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   工具：画文字（有 SDL_ttf 用纹理，否则用小点阵占位）
──────────────────────────────────────────────── */
static void draw_text(SDL_Renderer *ren, int x, int y,
                      const char *text, SDL_Color color)
{
#ifdef HAVE_SDL_TTF
    if (!g_font) return;
    SDL_Surface *surf = TTF_RenderUTF8_Blended(g_font, text, color);
    if (!surf) return;
    SDL_Texture *tex = SDL_CreateTextureFromSurface(ren, surf);
    SDL_Rect dst = { x, y, surf->w, surf->h };
    SDL_FreeSurface(surf);
    if (!tex) return;
    SDL_RenderCopy(ren, tex, NULL, &dst);
    SDL_DestroyTexture(tex);
#else
    /* 没有 SDL_ttf：简单画一条代表文字的彩色矩形 */
    SDL_SetRenderDrawColor(ren, color.r, color.g, color.b, color.a);
    SDL_Rect r = { x, y, (int)(strlen(text) * 8), 16 };
    SDL_RenderFillRect(ren, &r);
    (void)text;
#endif
}

for i in $(seq 0 127); do
    if [ $i -eq 72 ]; then
        continue
    fi
    echo "gpio"$i
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/export 2>/dev/null
    echo out > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/direction 2>/dev/null
    echo "1"
    echo 1 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 1
    echo "0"
    echo 0 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 1
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/unexport 2>/dev/null
done
echo "done"

for i in $(seq 31 52); do
    if [ $i -eq 72 ]; then
        continue
    fi
    echo "gpio"$i
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/export 2>/dev/null
    echo out > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/direction 2>/dev/null
    echo "1"
    echo 1 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 0.5
    echo "0"
    echo 0 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 0.5
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/unexport 2>/dev/null
done
echo "done"


for i in $(seq 79 127); do
    echo "gpio"$i
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/export 2>/dev/null
    echo out > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/direction 2>/dev/null
    echo "1"
    echo 1 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 0.5
    echo "0"
    echo 0 > /sys/class/gpio/gpio$i/value 2>/dev/null
    sleep 0.5
    echo $i > /sys/class/gpio/unexport 2>/dev/null
done
echo "done"

#define UART2_BASE 0x20068000
#define UART_THR 0x00
#define UART_LSR 0x14
static void dbg_putc(char c)
{
    volatile unsigned char *uart =
        (volatile unsigned char *)UART2_BASE;

    while (!(uart[UART_LSR] & 0x20))
        ;

    uart[UART_THR] = c;
}
static void dbg_puts(const char *s)
{
    while (*s)
        dbg_putc(*s++);
}

uart1_base: 0x20064000

LCR |= (1 << 7);   // DLAB=1

DLL = xxx;
DLH = xxx;

LCR &= ~(1 << 7);  // DLAB=0

////////// uart1 ///////////////////////
 // DLAB=1
md.l 0x2006400c 1
2006400c: 00000000                               ....
mw.l 0x2006400c 0x80 1

// UART_DLL
md.l 0x20064000 1
mw.l 0x20064000 0x0d 1
//UART_DLH
md.l 0x20064004 1

// DLAB=0
md.l 0x2006400c 1
mw.l 0x2006400c 0x03 1

// 发送-接收回环
md.l 0x20064000 1
// send
mw.l 0x20064000 0x55 1
// LSR 等待：THRE = 1 TEMT = 1
md.l 0x20064014 1
// 读取
md.l 0x20064000 1



///////// uart 2 //////////////////////////

md.l 0x2006807c 1

 // DLAB=1
=> md.l 0x2006800c 1
2006800c: 00000003                               ....
mw.l 0x2006800c 0x83 1

// UART_DLL
md.l 0x20068000 1
//UART_DLH
md.l 0x20068004 1

 // DLAB=0
md.l 0x2006800c 1
mw.l 0x2006800c 0x03 1





UART_LSR
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x0014)
Line Status Register




UART_DLL
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x0000)
Divisor Latch (Low)

7:0 RW 0x00
baud_rate_divisor_L
Lower 8-bits of a 16-bit, read/write, Divisor
Latch register that contains the baud rate
divisor for the UART. This register may only be
accessed when the DLAB bit (LCR[7]) is set
and the UART is not busy (USR[0] is zero).
The output baud rate is equal to the serial
clock (sclk) frequency divided by sixteen
times the value of the baud rate divisor, as
follows: baud rate = (serial clock frequency) /
(16 * divisor).
Note that with the Divisor Latch Registers
(DLL and DLH) set to zero, the baud clock is
disabled and no serial communications occur.
Also, once the DLH is set, at least 8 clock
cycles of the slowest UART clock should be
allowed to pass before transmitting or
receiving data.


UART_DLH
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x0004)
Divisor Latch (High)
7:0 RW 0x00
baud_rate_divisor_H
Upper 8 bits of a 16-bit, read/write, Divisor
Latch register that contains the baud rate
divisor for the UART.

md.l 0x2000000c 1

mw.l 0x2000000c 0x55 1

UART_LCR
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x000c)
Line Control Register
7 RW 0x0
div_lat_access
Divisor Latch Access Bit.
Writeable only when UART is not busy
(USR[0] is zero), always readable. This bit is
used to enable reading and writing of the
Divisor Latch register (DLL and DLH) to set the
baud rate of the UART. This bit must be
cleared after initial baud rate setup in order to
access other registers.


md.l 0x2006807c 1
UART_USR
Address: Operational Base + offset (0x007c)
UART Status Register

0 RO 0x0
uart_busy
UART Busy.
UART Busy. This is indicates that a serial
transfer is in progress, when cleared indicates
that the UART is idle or inactive.
1’b0:UART is idle or inactive
1’b1:UART is busy (actively transferring data)

config DEBUG_UART_ALWAYS
	bool "Always use debug UART mode"
	default y if !ROCKCHIP_PX5
	help
	  Say y to always use debug UART, skip complicated console UART register.



#define UCLASS_DRIVER(__name)						\
	ll_entry_declare(struct uclass_driver, __name, uclass)


#define ll_entry_declare(_type, _name, _list)				\
	_type _u_boot_list_2_##_list##_2_##_name __aligned(4)		\
			__attribute__((unused,				\
			section(".u_boot_list_2_"#_list"_2_"#_name)))

u-boot-next-dev\common\board_f.c

//////////////////

void board_init_f(ulong boot_flags)
{
	gd->flags = boot_flags;
	gd->have_console = 0;
	// int r1 = readl(0x2000007c);
	// printf("DM:    r1 = 0x%08x\n", r1);
	// printf("DM:    0x2006400c = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x2006400c));


	// printf("DM:    0x20064000 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064000));
	writel(0x80, 0x2006400c);
	// printf("DM:    0x20064000 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064000));
	writel(0x0d, 0x20064000);
	// printf("DM:    0x20064004 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064004));
	// printf("DM:    0x2006400c = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x2006400c));
	writel(0x03, 0x2006400c);
	printf("DM:    0x20064000 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064000));
	writel(0x55, 0x20064000);
	printf("DM:    0x20064014 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064014));
	printf("DM:    0x20064000 = 0x%08x\n", readl(0x20064000));

	if (initcall_run_list(init_sequence_f))
		hang();

#if !defined(CONFIG_ARM) && !defined(CONFIG_SANDBOX) && \
		!defined(CONFIG_EFI_APP) && !CONFIG_IS_ENABLED(X86_64)
	/* NOTREACHED - jump_to_copy() does not return */
	hang();
#endif
}

然后找到这段： 	

exitCode = runCommand(cmd)
改成：
# kill ES before launching emulator to free GPU
            import subprocess as _sp
            import time as _time
            # kill the watchdog script first (it's a bash process)
            _sp.run("pkill -9 -f emulationstation-standalone", shell=True, capture_output=True)
            _sp.run(["killall", "-9", "emulationstation"], capture_output=True)
            _time.sleep(2)
            exitCode = runCommand(cmd)
            # restart ES after emulator exits
            _sp.Popen(["/usr/bin/emulationstation-standalone"])

python3 << 'EOF'
with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = '            exitCode = runCommand(cmd)'
new = '''            import subprocess as _sp
            import time as _time
            _sp.run("pkill -9 -f emulationstation-standalone", shell=True, capture_output=True)
            _sp.run(["killall", "-9", "emulationstation"], capture_output=True)
            for _ in range(20):
                r = _sp.run("pgrep -f emulationstation", shell=True, capture_output=True)
                if r.returncode != 0:
                    break
                _time.sleep(0.5)
            _time.sleep(1)
            exitCode = runCommand(cmd)
            _sp.Popen(["/usr/bin/emulationstation-standalone"])'''

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new, 1)
    with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print("Done")
else:
    print("ERROR: target string not found")
EOF



python3 << 'EOF'
with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = '            _time.sleep(1)\n            exitCode = runCommand(cmd)'
new = '''            _time.sleep(1)
            _sp.run(["modprobe", "-r", "mali"], capture_output=True)
            _time.sleep(1)
            _sp.run(["modprobe", "mali"], capture_output=True)
            _time.sleep(1)
            exitCode = runCommand(cmd)'''

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new, 1)
    with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print("Done")
else:
    print("ERROR: not found")
EOF


python3 << 'EOF'
with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = '            for _ in range(20):'
new = '''            import os
            os.system("ps aux | grep -iE 'emulation' >> /tmp/es_kill.log 2>&1")
            for _ in range(20):'''

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new, 1)
    with open('/usr/lib/python3.11/site-packages/configgen/emulatorlauncher.py', 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print("Done")
else:
    print("ERROR: not found")
EOF

buildroot:
重新编译某个包：
make <pkg>-reconfigure
例如：
make openssl-reconfigure



make rk3128-pkg PKG=uboot-ps7000-rebuild
make rk3128-pkg PKG=uboot-ps7000-reconfigure
make rk3128-pkg PKG=uboot-ps7000-dirclean


| 修改内容                       | 推荐命令                | 是否重新 configure |
| -------------------------- | ------------------- | -------------- |
| 修改源码                       | `<pkg>-rebuild`     | ❌              |
| 修改 `.mk`（configure 参数、依赖等） | `<pkg>-reconfigure` | ✅              |
| 修改 patch、版本、下载地址、源码目录等     | `<pkg>-dirclean`    | 从头开始           |

修改uboot的下载地址，重新编译
make rk3128-pkg PKG=uboot-txcz-rk3128-v3-1-dirclean
make rk3128-pkg PKG=uboot-txcz-rk3128-v3-1
